Commentary

A Retrospective and Prospective Look at the Pacific International Academic Conference - Bin 50

(I) The Temporality of the Pacific Ocean

Former US President Roosevelt once said: "The Mediterranean era has long disappeared with the discovery of the Americas. The Atlantic era is also reaching its peak today and will soon exhaust all its vitality. Only the Pacific era is just dawning, and it will be the greatest era in ancient and modern times. This is due to the destiny of the times." In these few words, the temporality of the Pacific Ocean is fully expressed, as is the seriousness of the Pacific issue. The lightheartedness of the powerful is a symbol of the infinite storms that will occur on the Pacific Ocean in the future. Roosevelt's praise and admiration for the Pacific Ocean is precisely to confirm the great calamity of the Pacific's future.

Why will the Pacific Ocean be the greatest era in the future? In a word, after the imperialist powers have completed the division of colonies and markets on the Mediterranean and Atlantic Oceans, the markets and resources of the weak and small nations on the Pacific Ocean will rapidly become the target of competition and plunder by the powers. Therefore, the so-called greatest era of the Pacific Ocean is no different from saying that the Pacific Ocean will enter a serious era of competition and rivalry among the powers. However, is the arrival of this great era really "due to the destiny of the times," as Roosevelt said?

Since the end of the European War, which dissected the European colonies, the imperialist powers have obtained a temporary balance. At the same time, because of the fatigue of the war, all the imperialist powers needed a full rest. As a result, the world situation was able to remain temporarily at peace for a while. In the four or five years after the war, the imperialist powers achieved renewed prosperity, especially the United States and Japan, which leaped forward by leaps and bounds, reaching the highest peak of capitalism. The day of the renewed prosperity of capitalism is also the time when market problems and colonial problems re-emerge. The Pacific Ocean has extremely rich uncultivated raw materials and extremely vast undeveloped markets and investment sites. It is the inevitable destiny for it to become the target of the second competition among the powers. Recent people say that the Pacific issue has the same serious nature as the Mediterranean issue, which caused the first European War, and is a powder keg for future wars. Their words are almost accurate and appropriate.

The core of the Pacific issue, that is, the crux of the Pacific issue, is: first, the China issue; second, the immigration issue; and third, the raw materials and market issue. China has 4 million square miles of land, contains unlimited undeveloped resources, and has a population of one-quarter of the world's population, enough to serve as a market for the surplus products of the imperialist powers and as a great resource land for them to take from endlessly. Therefore, the China issue can almost be said to be the most central issue of the Pacific issue. Secondly, in recent times, various countries have suffered greatly from overpopulation. Governments have instead encouraged population growth, and the population has increased even more. Japan has an extremely small land area, and its population is already dense. However, according to the 1930 statistics, its population in the mainland was 64,447,000, and with Korea, Taiwan, and Sakhalin, it totaled 90,400,000, an increase of more than 6,945,000 compared to 1925, an annual increase of about one million people, which makes the problem of overpopulation even more acute. It has no choice but to emigrate abroad. However, looking around the world, the United States has already promulgated immigration laws in the East, and Australia has raised the slogan of "Australia for white people" in the South. Australia is again threatening China and Japan's increased power in the Pacific. Is this something the other powers are willing to accept? Therefore, the immigration issue is another difficult issue that causes disputes in the Pacific. Furthermore, countries such as China, India, Australia, and New Zealand in the Pacific are still stuck in the stage of agricultural economy, with extremely backward industries. The various unexploited raw materials are almost countless. The world's advanced industrial countries are feeling the accumulation of products and the panic of raw materials, and it is inevitable that they will rise up to seize them. Therefore, the issue of raw materials and markets is even more likely to cause disputes in the Pacific. In short, the Mediterranean issue is the past model of the Pacific issue. The first battle that the Mediterranean issue caused is no different from the preview of the world war that is about to be caused by the Pacific issue. The Pacific is about to become the greatest era in ancient and modern times, and it is made by people, not by destiny. Roosevelt's words are just a boast or joke made by the powerful, which is enough to give the weak and small nations of the world infinite terror and threats.

The countries surrounding the Pacific Ocean are numerous and complex. Countries such as Mexico, Peru, Chile, Panama, and Annam are insignificant and do not have a place on the field of Pacific competition. In fact, the only countries with the power to influence the situation on the Pacific Ocean and have the power to compete for hegemony on the Pacific Ocean are Britain, Japan, and the United States. Before the European War, Britain had already established a special force in the Far East. The Yangtze River basin in our country has long been regarded as a sphere of influence, and other countries are not allowed to shake it at all. Moreover, the British imperialists cannot allow other countries to take away the crown of maritime hegemony. It will not relax its competition on the Pacific issue at all. The United States benefited from the European War and is the world's largest wealthy country. The accumulation of capital and goods urgently needs to be exported abroad, and it has no choice but to ask for a share of the vast market in the Far East. Roosevelt once said, "Our future history will be determined by the Pacific Ocean facing China more than by the Atlantic Ocean facing Europe." Its ambition can be seen in general. As for Japan, although its national power has increased sharply due to the European War and it has jumped into the ranks of modern industrial countries, its country is uniquely thin. It feels extremely short of raw materials. The lack of iron and coal is its fatal injury. To save its national lifeline, it will spare no effort to seize raw materials. However, looking around the world, it cannot extend its iron hooves into the United States, nor can it raise its demonic claws to attack Europe. Only China, which has a vast territory and abundant resources on the Pacific Ocean, is the closest and most cowardly and deceitful. Therefore, it decided on a continental policy and actively advanced into the northeast of our country. At the same time, Japan is actually located on the Pacific Ocean. Its national power is strong and its military is sufficient. It will not allow others to encroach on its territory. How can others be allowed to sleep soundly next to the bed? The crown of

Page 8

Pacific hegemony will never be handed over to others. With these three countries as the center, and with the complex relationships of other countries in the world pushing and agitating, the Pacific Ocean is undergoing a transformation, with dangerous waves increasing day by day.

(To be continued)

Important News

Another Money Shortage is About to Occur in Liaoning Province 51

Shenyang Correspondence: The most complicated monetary system in the country is none other than that of Liaoning Province, with silver dollars, national currency notes, Fengtian dollars, Fengtian small dollars, dollar corner notes, decimal copper coins, and so on, a motley array that makes it difficult for newcomers to know how to use them. The most unmanageable thing in Liaoning Province is the Fengtian currency note. Although the history of the Fengtian currency note is very short, the drastic changes over the years are rare in the history of the monetary system. When it was first issued, it was called the one or two Fengtian dollar note, that is, each Fengtian dollar was exchanged for one dollar and two cents of Fengtian small dollars. At that time, the Fengtian dollar note was no different from the silver dollar, and residents used it as the standard for saving money. Some even considered the current dollar and the banknotes issued by the Bank of Communications to be unreliable and specialized in hoarding Fengtian currency notes as foolproof. When Wang Yongjiang was the head of the Department of Finance, he was still able to maintain credit and do his best to maintain it. Later, due to the heavy military use, banknotes were issued, and the Fengtian currency note reserve was very weak, and banknotes were issued endlessly. The market price of Fengtian currency notes gradually declined. However, as of the first half of the 17th year of the Republic of China, the lowest price was still only about 30 Fengtian dollars per silver dollar, and residents who hoarded Fengtian currency notes had already suffered a loss of two-thirds. Merchants used Fengtian currency notes for transactions. To take care of the cost, they had to raise prices as much as possible. The higher the prices, the lower the price of Fengtian currency notes. From the winter of the 17th year to the spring of the 18th year, the price of Fengtian currency notes fell to more than 60 yuan. The market was panicked, and merchants and people cried out in pain. Those who were impoverished and bankrupt were heard of every day, and small vendors and coolies were unable to maintain themselves. Those who were short-sighted and committed suicide were even more countless. The authorities, seeing that the situation was like this, if they did not try their best to maintain it, they were afraid that serious disturbances would occur. On the one hand, the legal price was strictly set, with 50 Fengtian dollars, that is, 60 Fengtian small dollars, worth one silver dollar. The salaries of government employees, merchants' trade, and farmers' taxes were all based on this standard, and no low or high was allowed. On the other hand, the central government was asked to approve the issuance of 18 million yuan of Liaoning Province's financial consolidation public bonds in the 18th year. Since this regulation, the market has begun to calm down. In the past two or three years, bank transactions have been able to maintain the legal price, and the difference is only one or two yuan. However, it can only be low or high in secret and dare not openly break the legal price. Even before the Lunar New Year this year, it was rumored that Fengtian currency notes would fall. The reporter went to various money houses to inquire about the market price of Fengtian currency notes. It was said that whether the price would fall or not could not be predicted, but if there were no special circumstances, it should not fall for no reason. However, recently, Fengtian currency notes suddenly fell sharply. According to the daily market of the Dongsan Province Official Silver Bank, although there were also falls and no rises, it was not drastic. On the 25th, it was 64 yuan and 20 cents, on the 26th, it was 64 yuan and 80 cents, and yesterday (27th) it was 65 yuan and 40 cents. However, the money houses' habit is not to use the market price set by the bank as the transaction standard. In recent days, the market price of money houses has been very different from that of the Official Silver Bank. Yesterday morning, it had fallen to 68 yuan, and in the afternoon, it continued to fall to 72 yuan. At the time of closing the market, it was even heard that it had fallen to 80 yuan. Most money merchants still do not easily sell cash. Today is Sunday, and there is no market as usual. However, the trend is uncertain, and it is difficult to predict whether it can be stabilized tomorrow. This tragic fall of Fengtian currency notes is the second blow since the 17th year. The reason for this is nothing more than the destruction of traitors. However, the citizens are talking about the tiger, and they have been running around to tell each other, as if a great disaster is coming. The sharp fall in three or five days is like a sudden storm, which is also an unprecedented phenomenon in the history of Fengtian currency notes. Now, Chairman Zang of the provincial government has joined the Department of Finance to strictly investigate the traitors who are destroying the market and punish them according to the law. On the one hand, he is quickly planning a stabilization strategy to restore the original state in the shortest possible time. (28th)

The Pinghan Transportation Will Be Restored Soon 52

The Road Administration Asks the Provincial Government to Strictly Prohibit Villagers from Digging Roads

Hankou Correspondence: South of Yancheng on the Pinghan Road, the bridge was submerged due to the rise of the Luohe River. At the same time, villagers dug roads to release the flood, and the Pinghan transportation was interrupted for five days. According to the Road Administration, the flood has receded, and all the projects have been rushed to repair by the Engineering Department overnight, and the entire road transportation can be restored on the 5th. All the first and second special express trains on the Pinghan Line will also depart as usual on the morning of the 5th. In addition, the Pinghan Road Management Committee believes that the traffic obstruction this time was caused by the flooding of the bridge, but the villagers digging roads to release the flood was also a major reason. On the 4th, it sent letters to the governments of Hubei, Henan, and Hebei provinces, ordering their subordinates to strictly prohibit it. The letter said, "According to the report of the Engineering Department of this road, a letter from Liu Hongjun, the chief of the second section of this road, to the police section chiefs of Shunyan and Yanhan, stated that now that the summer season has arrived, the rainy season has arrived, and in the past, villagers along the line often dug up road embankments to release water due to flooding, which has a very important impact on traffic. Measures should be taken to prohibit it to avoid damaging traffic. Please check and forward this to the county governments along the road, earnestly advise them, and issue strict prohibitions. This road's main embankment extends 1,414 kilometers. Every summer, when the rain is flooding, the above-mentioned excavation of road embankments to release water occurs from time to time. The section chief's letter to the two police section chiefs requesting that they forward it to the county governments along the road to strictly prohibit it is indeed an essential measure to maintain traffic. It should be submitted to you, asking you to forward it to the governments of Hebei, Henan, and Hubei provinces, and order all counties along the road to strictly prohibit villagers from digging up road embankments to release water in order to maintain traffic. In addition to sending separate letters, we are corresponding to request you to check and order all counties under your jurisdiction to strictly prohibit villagers from digging up road embankments to release water in order to maintain traffic." (July 4th)

Lu Zuo Inspects the Jinpu Railway 53

Negotiating Joint Transportation Methods with Various Railways

Tianjin Correspondence: Lu Zuo, Chairman of the Jinpu Railway Committee, arrived from Pukou to inspect the railway administration. He arrived in Tianjin at 7:00 AM this morning (3rd). Accompanying Lu were Chen Yongqing, Director of the Transportation Department; Yang Yi, Director of the Mechanical Department; Wu Xizhen, Director of the Engineering Department; Committee Member Qian Zongyuan; and more than ten attendants. All are staying at the National Hotel in the French Concession. At 9:00 AM, Lu visited Gao Jiyi, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau. At 10:00 AM, he went to the office to convene a meeting with staff and gave instructions. At 3:00 PM, he went to the Xigu Factory for inspection and convened a meeting with workers to give instructions. According to his remarks, his mission to the north includes: (1) Increasing the speed of express trains. The special express trains on the Jinpu Railway (Nos. 201 and 202) take 36 hours from Pukou to Tianjin, which is slower than the special express trains on the Jinghu and Beining Railways. The intention is to shorten the travel time for the convenience of passengers. However, the reason for the slow speed of trains on this railway is the years of war, disrepair of roads, damaged sleepers, and numerous bridges destroyed due to military operations. After the pacification of the military, the bridges were hastily repaired for traffic. For the sake of travel safety, the speed was not dared to be increased. Recently, the Engineering Department reported that the bridge repairs were completed at the end of June, so a personal inspection is necessary to ensure safety. However, the decay of sleepers is a major concern for traffic safety. 150,000 sleepers have been purchased for gradual replacement. This afternoon, I briefly discussed shortening the travel time with Gao Jiyi, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau. We will have a more detailed discussion tomorrow. After I return to Beijing, it can be implemented, and the Jinpu line will take about 24-25 hours to restore its old appearance. (2) Implementing joint transportation. After reorganization, this railway now has more than 70 locomotives and more than 900 passenger and freight cars. Although this is not enough to fully supply transportation needs, it is still barely sufficient. However, there are still more than 20 locomotives that need to be repaired at the Pukou factory before they can be used. Recently, eight new locomotives have been ordered from England, which are expected to arrive in Pukou around November of this year. This railway is a major north-south artery, but goods from the Longhai, Jiaoji, and Beining Railways cannot be transferred. This not only increases the cost of handling but also wastes time and labor, which is extremely inconvenient for merchants. This trip north is also a convenient opportunity to discuss joint transportation methods with the Longhai, Jiaoji, and Beining Railways. If this matter can be implemented, not only will the various railways benefit each other, but merchants will also benefit greatly. (3) Eliminating transport companies. This railway has thirty to forty transport companies of various sizes, who control the vehicles and make things difficult for passengers and merchants, preventing merchants from directly requesting cars from the railway bureau to transport goods. They have to beg the transport companies, who then treat the goods as rare commodities. Without paying a considerable price, one cannot obtain a railcar. Outsiders are unaware of this and mistakenly believe that the railway bureau is bribed to sell railcars. This bureau has been unjustly wronged, which is not worthwhile. Therefore, the transport companies will be abolished, effective from the first of this month. In the future, merchants can contact the nearest stationmaster to request cars to transport goods. As long as there are cars, they can be loaded at any time, reducing the suffering of merchants. As for the more than 700,000 yuan in security deposits paid by the transport companies, plus interest, totaling more than 800,000 yuan, due to the dilapidated state of this railway, it has been decided to refund it in three installments. (4) On the 30th of last month, I, along with the directors of various departments, took the 202 train from Pukou north. At 9:00 AM on the 1st, we arrived in Xuzhou, got off the train to inspect, and discussed joint transportation methods with Qian Zongze, Director of the Longhai Railway Bureau. Qian is the Vice Minister of the Ministry of Railways, so there are no problems with this matter. That evening at 8:00 PM, we took the second train north. At 9:00 AM on the 2nd, we arrived in Jinan and immediately discussed joint transportation with representatives of the Jiaoji Railway, which also resulted in a considerable agreement. At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, we went to the Jinpu Factory for inspection and convened a meeting with staff to give instructions. At 6:00 PM in the evening, we took the 202 train north again. Tomorrow, we will discuss joint transportation matters in detail with the Beining Railway. After returning to Beijing, we will make a comprehensive plan with various railways, and joint transportation can be implemented. The Bengbu Bridge, Guzhen Bridge, Dawen River Bridge, and Luokou Bridge on this railway, which were damaged by military operations, have all been repaired and are now strong. The organization of the railway union on this railway is not very sound. I think it is necessary to improve it. The Jinpu Railway ferry floating bridge is still actively underway. However, recently, there has been continuous summer rain in the south, and the river has risen sharply, slightly halting the bridge construction on the riverbank. It is expected that it will be fully completed in March or April next year. After the completion of this bridge, not only will travel be convenient, but goods from the north and south can directly reach their destinations, eliminating the hassle of loading and unloading on both sides of the Yangtze River. This railway is currently in a slow season, with monthly revenue of about one million yuan and annual revenue of about twenty million yuan. With continued efforts in reorganization, increasing locomotives, and adjusting transportation capacity, it is expected that annual revenue can reach thirty million yuan. (July 3)

The Remaining Bandits in Pingjiang, Hunan Province, Will Soon Be Eliminated 54

Wang Dongyuan Encourages Those Who Were Coerced to Renounce Banditry

Changsha Correspondence: The red bandits in Pingjiang, Hunan Province, have been suppressed repeatedly under the supervision of Wang Dongyuan of the 15th Division. The bandits have fled to the Jiangxi border in droves, and the villages are gradually becoming stable. Unexpectedly, on the 12th of this month, several thousand remnants of Kong Hechong's troops fled to the area. They were met head-on by Wang's troops, who killed one fake division commander and two fake regimental commanders, and captured many guns and bandits. The bandits died in droves in the fields. The intensity of the battle was unprecedented in the county's bandit suppression efforts. The bandits suffered a major blow this time, and their strength has been extinguished. The remnants are still fleeing to the Jiangxi border and are currently being cleared step by step. They will be completely eliminated in a few days. However, the bandits have been entrenched in this county for the longest time, and the people have been deeply banditized. Commander Wang now believes that since the core bandits have been pacified, those who were coerced can be forgiven. After repeated announcements, they are allowed to renounce banditry. Now, during the step-by-step suppression, a proclamation is re-issued, urging them to renounce banditry and surrender to avoid perishing with the bandits. The proclamation is as follows: This division has been ordered to station in Pingjiang to suppress bandits for half a year. At first, because the order was newly established, the people were under the coercion of the Communist bandits, and many were forced to join the bandits. Therefore, we treated them with leniency and did not investigate those who were coerced, allowing them to renounce banditry and opening a path to life. We have repeatedly issued orders and earnestly advised them, which should be known to all fathers, elders, brothers, sisters, aunts, and sisters in Pingjiang. On the 12th of this month, the bandit Kong Hechong reassembled a large number of bandits to attack our division's village defense, attempting a final struggle. Our Li Regiment fiercely attacked them, killing more than a thousand bandits, seizing hundreds of guns, and scattering them in all directions, collapsing into disarray. In total, in the battles of Longmen, Pingjiang, Shicun, and others, the Kong bandits were repeatedly defeated, and their strength disintegrated, making them unable to withstand a single blow, which can be seen in general. This division is currently joining forces with Chen's Division in Liuyang and Tan's Division in Xiutong to encircle and suppress the Kong bandits, which is imminent. At this opportunity, you, the people, should intensify your efforts to help our army, scout out bandit information, search for bandit dens, and cooperate between the army and the people to quickly achieve the effect of clearing the entire territory. If there are still those who are obstinate or have lingering intentions, they must lead their sons, supervise their brothers, and urge them to renounce banditry or tie them up and send them here, which will be dealt with leniently, so as not to perish with the bandits, causing grief to your parents and brothers. This division commander, in the past, was concerned about those who were coerced and had the suffering of being forced to join the bandits, and did not hesitate to speak earnestly, repeatedly urging them to renounce banditry and return to goodness, truly embodying the virtue of heaven and earth's love for life, and not just being able to kill. Now, because the time has been long, it is not appropriate to be overly concerned, so that the chief villains have been subjected to public execution for a long time. Therefore, this proclamation is made in good faith. After this announcement, if there are still riots, disturbances, or work for the bandits in Pingjiang, it is truly self-generated and willing to become bandits. We will resolutely use the principle of killing to stop killing, adopt the final means, carry out a bloodbath, and leave no grass behind. Do not say that you were not warned. Let everyone be vigilant, be careful with this proclamation.

The Progress of Disaster Relief in Hunan Province 55

The Relief Association Sends Letters to All Sectors in Shanghai and Hankou for Assistance

And Asks the Changjun Guild Hall to Quickly Remit the Previously Raised Relief Funds

Changsha Correspondence: The Hunan Disaster Relief Association believes that the flood in Hunan Province this time is extremely severe, unprecedented in recent decades. Although it has been decided to issue Hunan disaster relief public bonds of three million yuan to provide relief, due to the importance of the matter, it cannot be completed in a short time, and the starving are waiting for relief, which cannot be delayed. The association has also established a Hunan Disaster Relief Association and a Fundraising Committee in Hankou to raise large sums of money in the prosperous commercial ports of Shanghai and Hankou to provide emergency relief. In order to ensure the smooth progress of the association's affairs, it has sent letters to all sectors for assistance. At the same time, it has sent a letter to the Changjun Guild Hall in Hankou, asking it to quickly remit the funds raised previously to Hunan to save the dying. The letters are recorded on the left.

Letter to Various Groups in Shanghai and Hankou: Respectfully, Hunan has suffered from years of war and has not yet recovered. The red flames are rampant and still fierce. Recently, the counties along the Xiang River have been flooded. In the counties along the river, mountain torrents have erupted, turning houses into ruins and fields into nothing. Livestock, grain, food, silver, and money have all been swept away by the floods. The disaster in dozens of counties is unprecedented in recent decades and is rare in more than twenty provinces. Seeing this strange disaster, the members of our association are deeply worried. We have organized the Hunan Disaster Relief Association, which was established on the 8th of this month. It has been submitted to the Hunan Provincial Party Affairs Guidance Committee and the Hunan Provincial Government for filing. At the same time, we have submitted a request to the provincial government to issue disaster relief public bonds of three million yuan, with the remaining profits from the Shuikoushan as collateral, which has also been approved. However, disaster relief is urgent and requires immediate action. The fundraising method cannot be limited to established practices. In addition to the government members setting up a Disaster Relief Bond Raising Bureau in Hankou to solicit merchants to find ways to promote sales, the starving are waiting for relief, which cannot be delayed. Our association has also publicly recommended Luo Junduo and Shu Junlijian to set up a Hunan Disaster Relief Association and a Fundraising Committee in Hankou to raise large sums of money in the prosperous commercial ports of Shanghai and Hankou to provide emergency relief. We have always believed that your association is kind, eager to help others, and concerned about the disaster in Hunan. We hope that you will give us your strong support to save the lives of more disaster victims and create more happiness for the people of Hunan. Not only will the members of the open association be grateful, but also we will look forward to your reply. We wish you well.

Letter to the Changjun Guild Hall in Hankou: Respectfully, the disaster in Hunan is tragic, unprecedented, and unimaginable. The newspapers have revealed it, and the public has spread the news. We believe that all gentlemen are concerned about their hometowns and have a clear understanding of the situation. However, the red flames in Hunan are still rampant. Chaling and Anren have just been recovered, but then the county was lost again. The suffering in the depths of water and fire is unbearable. Now, after this great flood, the survivors have no way to survive, the dead have no time to be buried, and they are displaced and exposed, which is truly unbearable to describe. It is found that the flood in Hunan Province in 1926 was also severe. The gentlemen of the overseas compatriots in Hankou raised more than 10,000 yuan in relief funds, which were stored for allocation. Later, it was suspended due to an incident and has not been remitted to Hunan. We believe that it is still preserved and has not been moved. This year's disaster in Hunan is a hundred times more severe than that of 1926. Our colleagues have no hesitation in organizing the Hunan Disaster Relief Association and want to do our best to raise relief funds. Now, we are pleading for the lives of hundreds of thousands of disaster victims. We hope that you will give us your strong support and quickly remit the funds raised previously to Hunan to save the lives of these dying people. We are extremely hopeful. Our association has publicly recommended Luo Junduo, the director of the investigation department, and Shu Lijian, the director of the design department, to come to Hankou to listen to your instructions in person. We hope that you will give us instructions on everything. We are extremely grateful.

The Torrential Rains in the Three Rivers of Guangdong Province 56

The Guangzhou-Shaoguan Train Stopped Due to a Landslide

The Banks of the Three Rivers Have All Become Swamps

Guangzhou Correspondence: The torrential rains in the East, West, and North Rivers of Guangdong Province have suddenly risen at the same time. Since June 28, the floods have spread to both banks of the Pearl River. The streets near the embankments in Guangzhou City that have not closed the roads have all been flooded, with a depth of about one foot. The low-lying inner streets in the Xiguan area have also become swamps. The river water in the provincial river has turned into a bloody red, and the water is turbulent, making it extremely dangerous to travel by boat. According to yesterday's report on the river water, there has been continuous rain in the North River, and mountain torrents have suddenly arrived. On the 28th, the area near the military field station to Yuantan station on the Yue-Shao Railway was flooded by mountain torrents, and the villagers rushed to escape. At the Lidong station near Yingde, a barren mountain with loose soil was eroded by rainwater and collapsed more than half on the morning of the 28th. The mud and stones crushed about three feet of the track at Lidong station, and all the utility poles and wires were destroyed. It was also reported that from midnight to 3:00 AM this morning, the loess mountain, also known as the Bolo Gang, near the Bopotang on the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway was hit by mountain rain and suddenly collapsed, covering the track with mud and soil, covering an area of about one or two acres. More than ten feet of the track sleepers from the Pa River estuary to the Bopotang station were destroyed. When the station staff heard the alarm, they urgently telegraphed Shaoguan to stop the southbound passenger and freight trains and simultaneously telegraphed the Huangsha main station to stop the northbound trains. Therefore, the second passenger and freight train from Guangzhou to Shaocheng on that day returned after reaching the Pa River estuary and did not arrive until after midnight. On the 29th, the tracks at each station above Yuantan were still submerged by the floodwater, and the train could not run. To this day, the direct express train from Guangzhou to Shaoguan has been suspended for three days. Areas from Yuantan to the Pa River estuary, Hengshi, and other places have become swamps, and the villagers nearby have been displaced. Several sections of the embankments around the Pa River have collapsed, and countless houses have collapsed, and countless people and livestock have drowned. Moreover, the Pa River flows directly to Qingyuan County, so the county's floods are even more severe. It is estimated that there have been reports of embankment collapses every day since the 25th. The Rongshu Village embankment in the county, which is the largest embankment, also collapsed on the 26th, and all the residents of the village drowned. The highway from Qingyuan to Yinzhan'ao was also washed away by the water. The county has sent a representative to the province to request relief. As for the floodwater in the West River, according to a returning guest from Wuzhou, the streets of Wuzhou on the 28th were about two feet deep, and boats could travel on land. Because Zhaoqing has a gorge, the water is particularly turbulent, and the overturning of boats is heard every day. The floodwater in Yuecheng has risen by more than ten feet, especially at the Lianjiang River estuary. The height of the floodwater can be level with the door lintels of the shops. Residents built floating bridges to come and go and moved to the foothills to live temporarily at night. The southwest of Sanshui is the confluence of the Northwest and West Rivers. Currently, the streets in the southwest are knee-deep in water, and residents use small boats as a means of transportation. Most of the goods are moved to the embankments for trade. The inner streets of Foshan are shin-deep in water. Since the 29th, merchants and residents have built floating bridges to come and go. As for the East River, there has been heavy rain every day since the beginning of summer. The water level of the river has risen to eight feet, and the rice fields along the river have become a vast expanse of water. The early rice crops have already been lost. (July 1)

The Xuzhou Legal Groups Resolved on Measures to Deal with the Dike Protection Uprising 57

The Post-Disaster Committee for the June 30th Public Property Tragedy Was Established

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Xuzhou Dike Protection Uprising was properly resolved after a joint meeting of various legal groups at the county government at noon on the 3rd. More than 20 representatives attended the meeting that day, presided over by County Magistrate Yang Wei. After each representative discussed the items one by one, the following resolutions were made: (1) The name of this meeting is set as the "Post-Disaster Committee for the June 30th Public Property Tragedy in Tongshan County." (2) Measures to deal with the Jiudetang: A. The county government will abolish the Jiudetang according to law. B. The county government will declare the official property led by the Jiudetang invalid according to law. C. Severely punish the responsible personnel of the Jiudetang, such as Lan Tianyi. (3) Measures for condolence to the injured and dead civilians: A. The various organs and legal groups will raise donations to handle the condolence, and the amount is tentatively set at 300 yuan, which will be advanced by the Property Office. B. The fundraising matters will be handled by the county government, the Public Security Bureau, the county party headquarters, the chamber of commerce, and the first district office. C. The condolence matters will be handled by the party headquarters of the first and second districts, the relief institute, the education bureau, and the farmers' association. (4) Measures to punish Zuo Shuyu, Director of the Public Property Bureau: A. The local legal groups will jointly submit a letter to the provincial government and the Ministry of Civil Affairs and the Ministry of Finance, requesting punishment according to law. B. The legal groups will submit a letter to the county government to forward to the provincial government and the Ministry of Civil Affairs and the Ministry of Finance for handling according to law. (5) This committee will print a letter of comfort to the people and distribute it to the injured and dead civilians to comfort the people. (6) Organize a Tongshan County Local Public Property Review Committee to deal with public property issues, and recommend the county party headquarters, the county government, the farmers' association, the Public Security Bureau, the Construction Bureau, the Education Bureau, the party headquarters of the first and second districts, the first district branch office, the education association, and the chamber of commerce to serve as review members. (7) Release the detained civilians. After the discussion, the case has been concretely resolved and the meeting was adjourned. Today (4th), the responsible persons have been executing the resolutions separately. Except for Zhang Chuanyi, the township head of Yuanqiao, who has not yet been released, the remaining detained civilians have been released on bail. After the case occurred, the county government requested the Jinpu Railway Garrison Headquarters to issue a temporary martial law order. Commander Wang believed that the county government's measures for this case were inappropriate, and the issuance of martial law was not a military situation and was not approved. He instructed the county government to consider the public opinion and formulate a fair handling method and submit it to the competent authority for approval. He also ordered the military police inspection office to send more troops to patrol and pay attention to suppression at any time, peacefully stopping the matter, so as to avoid causing more incidents. (4th)

The Executive Yuan Did Not Approve the Establishment of Yantai as a City 58

Jinan Correspondence: The Executive Yuan previously believed that Yantai's population was less than 200,000 and did not have the qualifications to be established as a city. It ordered the cancellation of the Yantai Municipal Government and merged it into Fushan County. Subsequently, Liu Zhennian, a member of the Shandong Provincial Government and commander of the 21st Division, sent a letter to the provincial government, stating that Yantai was a place where Chinese and foreigners lived together, and there were many foreign affairs. It was inconvenient to handle matters without a municipal government. It was proposed to organize a small-scale municipal government and asked for a resolution. The provincial government meeting discussed the case and submitted it to the Ministry of Civil Affairs and the Ministry of Finance for review and sent it to the Executive Yuan for instructions, along with two alternative methods: (1) Establish a small-scale municipal government. (2) Expand the foreign affairs section of Fushan County. After the submission, the Executive Yuan submitted the case to the Ministry of the Interior for review, which still believed that Yantai was not suitable for establishment as a city. There were three reasons: (1) The population was less than 200,000. (2) Yantai was very close to Fushan County, which was not inconvenient in any way. (3) Yantai had not handled the licensing tax, etc. The Executive Yuan replied to Lu the day before yesterday. Today (3rd), the provincial government meeting raised it for discussion again and decided to inform Liu Zhennian of the Executive Yuan's reply. The issue of Yantai's establishment as a city has come to a temporary end. (3rd)

Qingdao Business Tax Collected Regularly 59

Collected in Four Installments Starting from July

Qingdao Correspondence: The Qingdao business tax was implemented by order of the central government to compensate for the loss of the abolition of likin. Preparations have been underway for several months. Various collection regulations, implementation rules, and tax rate tables have been stipulated earlier. However, because they have not been revised and approved by the Ministry of Finance, they have not been implemented for a while. The Ministry of Finance has revised them separately, submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval according to law, and telegraphed the Qingdao Municipal Government and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to comply. The municipal government has ordered the Finance Bureau to comply. It is reported that the Business Tax Collection Office has decided to implement the collection starting from July, in four installments per year, with three months as one installment, from July, August, and September of this year as the first installment. The investigation of the business situation of various merchants is about to be completed. The regulations of the Collection Office are recorded as follows: Article 1: In order to ensure that the city handles the business tax as a special responsibility, a Business Tax Collection Office is specifically established to manage it. Article 2: The Business Tax Collection Office (hereinafter referred to as this office) is attached to the Finance Bureau. Article 3: The collection of business tax by this office shall be handled in accordance with the city's business tax collection regulations and implementation rules. Article 4: This office shall have one director, who shall be appointed by the Municipal Government upon request from the Finance Bureau, subject to the supervision of the bureau director, and shall be in charge of all affairs of the office. Article 5: This office shall set up seven staff members according to the nature of the affairs, who shall be appointed by the Finance Bureau to be responsible for tasks such as inspection, ticket, investigation, and documents. Article 6: This office may use clerks as appropriate according to the complexity of the affairs. Article 7: The detailed rules of this office will be set separately. Article 8: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (July 1)

Bandits committed robbery and raped a young girl: Six bandits suddenly came to Chen Genfu's house in Zhongjiabang Village near Zhangliantang in the county's third district the night before last. He denied committing the robbery and only confessed that Zhang Hesheng raped Chen's daughter. The team is now strictly pursuing the fugitive bandits to bring them to justice.

After receiving the report, the regiment leader led his team to encircle and capture them. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already received information and ambushed in advance. Changshu 63

Three Bandits to be Sent to the Command Headquarters for Interrogation: The Sixth Company of the Provincial Security Team stationed in Ping, Changshu County, apprehended three bandits, Wang Fengyi, Chen Changwan, and Lu Rujin, in Hu on the 28th of last month. They were sent to the battalion headquarters, where Battalion Commander Shen interrogated them. Chen Changwan confessed to being a bandit and committing crimes in Hu and Shanghai, colluding with Lu Rujin and others in robberies, and acknowledging Wang Fengyi as their boss. Wang Fengyi, however, gave evasive statements, denying being a bandit. Lu Rujin even claimed to be a detective in the First Squad of the Thirteenth Team of the Water Police, and was bailed out by Yang Qingjiu, the captain of the Thirteenth Team. Subsequently, the Hu Pu North Goods Association and others deemed Captain Yang's action inappropriate and filed a complaint with the provincial government and the Security Bureau. Recently, Battalion Commander Shen Yiming went to inspect the Fuliang Bridge in Taicang, and incidentally learned that Wang Fengyi had committed crimes in Changshu during the Republic of China Year 15, and had fled to Taicang, colluding with ruffians and engaging in kidnapping. He was wanted by the defense corps and escaped. His son was captured and is still in jail. After Battalion Commander Shen completed a detailed investigation, he returned to Changshu. He has now decided to bring back Lu Rujin, who was bailed out by the Thirteenth Team, from Yang Qingjiu, and to re-interrogate him along with the temporarily detained Wang and Chen, before sending them to the Jiangyin Command Headquarters for interrogation.

Another Large-Scale Transfer of Police Officers: Since Yin Peng came to Changshu to take over as the director of the County Public Security Bureau, there have been numerous changes in the police officers and staff of the various branch offices. Public Security Bureau Disposes of Bandit Boats: The County Detective Team previously seized many bandit boats while cracking down on bandits in Liantang and other places. These boats are still docked in the city river behind the county government. Attempts to auction them off have been unsuccessful. Now, the Public Security Bureau, in handling summer sanitation, has hired many cleaners to remove garbage. However, with the large amount of garbage to be transported, more boats are needed. Wuxi 64

County Relief Institute Petitions for Subsidy: Yang Shoumei and Qin Ren Cun, the president and vice-president of the County Relief Institute, stated that according to a letter from Hua Wenchuan, the director of the institute's medical clinic, the clinic's funding is insufficient. The income and expenses of all the Hengshan assets are not enough to cover the costs. According to the resolution of the joint meeting, the allowance for the original 400 impoverished people must still be issued monthly and maintained as usual. However, the proposed budget expenditure of the medical clinic has no source of funding and requests to find ways to raise funds or ask the County Treasury to allocate funds to carry out the project. As for the election of Wenchuan as the director of the medical clinic, he believes he is unqualified and unable to take on the responsibility, and hopes to be removed by the county and appoint a virtuous and capable person, etc. After approving the letter, President Yang stated that the Hengshan assets were originally not much, and in the late Qing Dynasty, most of them relied on donations from the business community. In recent years, these donations have completely stopped, making it difficult to maintain the allowances for the 400 impoverished people, and now they are also undertaking medical work, and the expenditure has no source of funding, which is indeed the actual situation. However, since they have already undertaken to handle it, they cannot stop it due to lack of funding. In addition to instructing them to reduce the budget expenditure and merge the staff, they specially submitted a report to the county government yesterday, requesting to find ways to subsidize them so that they can work hard to carry out the project. As for Director Hua's resignation, a letter has been sent to earnestly retain him.

Recruiting Crew Members for Chartered Steamships, Crew Members Desert: The Transportation Department of the Nanjing Headquarters previously received a telegram from the Nanchang Commander-in-Chief's Office, requiring ten shallow-draft steamships to be chartered immediately. The department, upon receiving the order, dispatched commissioners Hua Shousong and others to Wuxi to contact the County Chamber of Commerce and the Shipping Association. Ten steamships, including Youdao, Shengli, and Wanli, were chartered and set sail for Nanjing on the first of this month. However, most of the crew members deserted en route, leaving the ships without drivers. The Transportation Department of the Headquarters, urgently needing the steamships due to repeated telegrams from the Nanchang Commander-in-Chief's Office, telegraphed the County Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday, requesting that they be responsible for equipping the ships with personnel, earnestly inform them, and order them to quickly return to their original ships to serve, or to supplement them as appropriate, to ensure that the ships' drivers and managers are fully equipped. After receiving the telegram, the County Chamber of Commerce repeatedly stated that the Wuxi steamships have a very shallow draft and are yacht-like in nature, making them difficult to withstand wind and waves. The machinery has been damaged and cannot be started. Yesterday, they specially telegraphed the Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, requesting that the Transportation Department be ordered to return them. At the same time, the County Chamber of Commerce also stated that recently, there have been bad elements in the outside world, falsely sealing ships and swindling, which is indeed hateful. They also sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, requesting that they be strictly prohibited to reassure the people and facilitate navigation.

Zhenjiang 67

Factory Owner Steals City Bricks: He San (aka He Bingsheng), the owner of the Heyuanji carpentry shop in Shuangjing Lane in the city, has accumulated a huge amount of wealth in recent years due to the relocation of the provincial government to Zhenjiang and repeated contracting of construction work on various agency buildings, often using means of cutting corners. Last year, he leased the land and buildings of the Hongqikou Banner People's Livelihood Office and planned to raise shares to open a Hongxing bathhouse. There have been repeated disputes. Later, the Bank of China established a branch and obtained a mortgage of 2,000 yuan to construct the brick wall, which contained a large number of city bricks. The Construction Engineering Office found out that He had never purchased city bricks and was suspected of theft. He was summoned for interrogation, but he was afraid to appear in court and asked someone to intercede. The office inquired in detail where the bricks came from, but He could not answer. Director Ye was very angry and immediately sent someone to summon He for severe punishment by the court. Hearing this, He fled and hid in the countryside temporarily. After someone spoke on his behalf, the office proposed a minimum penalty of 4,000 yuan to be confiscated and ordered that the stolen city bricks be returned. The matter is still under mediation.

The Finance Bureau Starts Collecting Land Value Tax: The Zhenjiang County Finance Bureau will collect the first installment of the land value tax for the 20th year of the Republic of China in three installments after transforming the string system. The first installment of the land value tax for the fields in all 17 districts, i.e., the original amount of the additional silver, should be collected urgently. The collection of the second and third installments of the land value tax will be announced after the autumn harvest is determined. Therefore, in addition to preparing the payment notices for the first installment of this year's land value tax and the second clean-up fee, and distributing them to the map administrators for distribution to each household for payment, the bureau specially set up a window at the bureau yesterday to start the collection.

The Department of Agriculture Requests an Extension of the Fishery Registration Period: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mines stated that the various fishery registration procedures have not yet been completed, and many county fishery associations have not been formally established. Moreover, pirates in various places have not been pacified, making it difficult to register all fishing boats. The stipulated deadline is approaching, and if it is cut off suddenly, there will be many omissions. Therefore, yesterday, it specially telegraphed the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting approval to extend the period by six months in order to handle it calmly.

The Captain of the Water Police Team was Assassinated: Xie Zezhi, the captain of the 18th Water Police Team stationed in Tong, was stabbed six times with a knife by Yan Zheming at the team headquarters at about 6 pm on the 3rd, injuring his left and right arms and left chest. He immediately called for help. The guards opened fire to protect him. Yan Zheming was captured after being injured. At about 11 pm, Yan Zheming took advantage of the guards' carelessness and escaped. He was shot and killed by the guards at the gate in front of the county court. He was immediately buried in the Eastern Common Cemetery. Captain Xie was taken to the Chengnan Hospital with a total of six wounds, bleeding heavily, but his life was not in danger. According to the team headquarters, Captain Xie was originally the captain of the Zhongshan warship, and Yan Zheming was his old subordinate. Yan came to Tong a month ago to ask Xie for a job but failed, so he harbored resentment. Xie gave him five yuan for travel expenses and told him to return to his hometown. Yan then took out a dagger and committed the crime. The injured Captain Xie is 32 years old, from Jiangxi, and has only been in office for less than three months.

Drowning While Swimming: Yesterday afternoon, Liu Dazhuizi, who lived by pulling a cart by the Chenghang River near the Wenchang Tower, took five or six children to the Niu Dawan River south of the Dahong Bridge in the Slender West Lake outside the North Gate of the city to swim and fish for mussels. Fire at Wujiahe Warehouse: The Wujia Tea and Food Shop on Lianqiao Main Street in this city has caught fire twice last month, but fortunately it did not spread. Female Singers Re-Impose Pure Song Tax: Bengbu female singers have always had a pure song tax. Now, the Public Security Bureau believes that it is necessary to restore the tax payment for female singers, and specially invoked the Anqing Entertainment Management Regulations to re-investigate the number of female singers, order them to register separately, and pay the pure song tax every month. Sino-American Extraterritoriality Negotiations 73

To be continued in China upon receipt of US documents

Regarding the Sino-American extraterritoriality negotiations, after Dr. Wu Chaoshu, our country's ambassador to the United States, resigned, the case has already been contacted by the US ambassador to China, Johnson, and Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, who decided to move the handling to China. However, the US ambassador is not very familiar with the content of the negotiations between the two parties in the United States and the extent to which they have reached, so he must wait for the US government to send all the negotiation documents to China before continuing. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Sound Society interviewed a certain important American official. According to him, the US government has already prepared all the negotiation documents, sealed them, and sent them to China. The package includes many things such as the exchange of notes and negotiation records between Ambassador Wu and the US diplomatic authorities, as well as the US side's opinions. It has already been sealed and sent to Shanghai. The US ambassador is expected to receive it around the end of this month or the beginning of next month. Once Mr. Johnson receives these documents, learns the details, and reads them in detail, he can go south to meet with Foreign Minister Wang and continue the negotiations.
