Municipal Chamber of Commerce Recommends Promoting Woolen Factory 75

Document presented to the Ministry of Industry

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce presented a document to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, saying, "Presenting for the purpose of presenting matters. The association held a general meeting of members on June 27. According to the proposal put forward by the Woolen Industry Association, our country has a vast land and abundant resources, with a population of 470 million. Production is declining, and we rely on foreigners for everything. What a shame. As far as the most important woolen goods are concerned, such as Zhigong woolen cloth, overcoat woolen cloth, and Huate woolen cloth, etc., today they have become essential items for the lives of our people. Almost all ordinary social clothes, hats, and shoes are made of woolen cloth. The annual imports are about 50 million taels of silver. For decades, we have not heard of any measures to set up factories to resist them. In recent years, although there are camel wool factories and one or two woolen factories with equipment, they are far from comparable to foreign factories. Moreover, the output is not much, and what they supply is less than one or two percent of what is needed. It is almost like using a cup of water to save a cart of firewood. Woolen cloth was invented in England. The raw material, wool, is mostly produced in Australia and Siberia. Occasionally, there is a small amount of research. Therefore, the output is inferior to that of Australia and West Asia. Otherwise, it is also a very good production in our country. According to the area where sheep are produced in Australia and West Asia and the place where woolen cloth is woven in England, the people who rely on it for their livelihoods are unknown. There is a place in England called Yorkshire, which is a concentrated area of woolen factories. The products, in addition to those used in the country, are all resold abroad by the export shops in Bradford.

Therefore, the people in these two places all live on woolen cloth, and few engage in other industries. Later, France invented a kind of plain serge, made of second-grade wool mixed with waste materials, which was cheaper than English cloth. Initially, there were only two or three small factories, but because it was widely sold in our country, it took the place of English cloth. (French plain serge, when imported into our country the most, amounted to more than 3,000 boxes per year.) Until today, its large and small serge factories have increased to dozens, and the sudden increase in productivity and the employment of workers all come from the gift of our Chinese people. Recently, Japan saw that French serge was selling well, so it also spun this type of serge. Every year, 800 to 1,000 boxes are imported into our country, but the output of French goods has not been affected in the slightest. In addition, there are also fancy woolen cloth, flat and thick woolen cloth, felt woolen cloth, etc., from Germany, Italy, and other countries, which are also a large number. This can prove that woolen cloth has become an essential item for the lives of our people in our country. Recently, the British, because serge has been taken away by France and Japan, spent more than 13,000 pounds (it is said that the Manchester Chamber of Commerce bears 30%, the local chambers of commerce 20%, and the government 50%) to send an economic survey team to China. Although the surface is to investigate cotton cloth, in fact, woolen cloth is also valued. The purpose is nothing more than to recover the old position. After returning to the country, they have united various woolen factories to form a large unity. The government is behind them, hoping to compete with France and Japan. All of these want to take our country as their market. They exhaust their efforts, absorb money, and design, using all means to the extreme. Therefore, members are frightened and want to save the situation. They must have sufficient equipment. They must know that saving the country through industry and relying on people's livelihoods cannot but be followed up urgently. The members sit idly by and watch tens of millions of dollars overflow every year. Every time they think of it, they want to organize a factory with a slightly larger scale, but because the required capital is too large, they cannot do it. Therefore, they will buy and sell its advantages and disadvantages at the general meeting in order to enable patriotic people to work together to carry out the project. How to take on its fixed capital and how the national power can be supplemented, and also ask to transfer it to the national government, and plan the day and night. The members rely on woolen cloth for their business, and they will not dare to fall behind in promoting domestic woolen cloth. If the government adopts it and orders the organization, the members are willing to work hard to promote it. The matter concerns the national economy and people's livelihood, and they propose that the association make a public decision and transfer it to the national government for adoption and implementation. The second article of the General's Outline for Founding the Country states that the government should seek the development of weaving with the people in order to enrich the people's clothing. Woolen fabrics are necessary for clothing. The existing factories have not prepared their products, and the number is limited. They are not enough to meet the needs of the people. In the past, the Gansu Weaving Factory and the Shanghai Weaving Bureau had precedents of raising funds from public companies. At a time when commercial capabilities are still in their infancy, the teachings of the General are followed from afar, and the success of various countries is taken as a model. Without the full cooperation of the government, it is impossible to develop domestic woolen fabrics and recover the overflow of profits. Based on the above reasons, the association members decided at the general meeting of members on June 27 to submit it to your ministry for adoption and implementation. The reason is to record the case and prepare a document for presentation. May your ministry examine it and approve its implementation.

Statistics on Machinery Industry Factories in the City 76

Investigation by the Statistical Office, Ministry of Industry, and other five agencies

The Daily News reported that the joint investigation by the Statistical Office of the National Government, the Ministry of Industry, and other five agencies has been extended to the end of this month. The office has now found that there are about 2,000 machinery industry factories in Shanghai, including 170 silk weaving factories, more than 30 silk weaving factories, more than 170 machinery factories, more than 100 silk factories, more than 30 textile factories, more than 30 foundry factories, more than 70 cloth factories, 100 printing factories, more than 40 tobacco industries, 40 rubber and rubber sound factories, and more than 40 hosiery departments.

Strictly Prohibit Raising Prices After Cutting Customs Duty 77

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Letter to Various Trade Associations

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent letters to various trade associations, saying, "Following the order of the Social Bureau and the Ministry of Industry, the Central Secretariat Office issued a letter stating that the Central Secretariat Office, under the direction of Jiang, the concurrent director, received a letter from the Hubei Provincial Party Headquarters requesting strict prohibition of merchants from raising prices after cutting customs duty. The order was handed over to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, etc. for reasons. The Central Government has clearly ordered the cutting of customs duty in order to consider the people's livelihood. Prices in various places should be low, which is enough to support the government's intention to cut customs duty. If merchants take the opportunity to raise prices, it is inappropriate. You should understand the local situation, strictly prohibit it, and report the handling situation at any time for verification." Therefore, a letter is hereby issued to inform you, please take note.

The Social Affairs Bureau Restricts Private Contracts Between Labor and Management 78

Agreements that conflict with group agreements are invalid.

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau announced yesterday that, in accordance with Article 16 of the Group Agreement Law, it is necessary to restrict labor contracts between employers and workers that differ from group agreements, because workers are ignorant and easily controlled, which is also the government's intention to protect labor. Now that the law has not yet been implemented, private contracts between labor and management in this city that differ from group agreements are not uncommon. Therefore, it is announced that the content of labor contracts between employers and workers that differ from the labor conditions stipulated in the group agreement are invalid. The invalid parts are replaced by the provisions of the group agreement. However, agreements that differ from the group agreement are valid if they are permitted by the group agreement or change labor conditions for the benefit of the workers and the group agreement does not expressly prohibit them. In addition, for group agreements with no time limit, the minimum time limit is set to one year. Even if it exceeds one

year and there is no new agreement, the labor contract should still be bound by it. All parties of labor and management in this city should abide by it.

All Businesses Should Join the Trade Association 79

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Requests Legal Mandate

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "Regarding the matter of making a request, the association held a members' general meeting on June 27th. According to the proposal submitted by the Cotton Fabric Trade Association, chambers of commerce in our country are, according to legal regulations, based on industrial and commercial trade associations as their fundamental organization, and industrial and commercial trade associations are based on individual businesses within the same industry as their fundamental organization. However, the legal provisions regarding participation in groups are all discretionary, leading to a wait-and-see attitude and hesitation. With members scattered and unorganized, a sound structure is difficult to achieve. With command not unified, how can strength be concentrated? It is difficult to effectively utilize commercial organizations to promote industrial and commercial development. Therefore, to correct these problems and solidify the foundation, it is proposed that this association request the government to make mandatory regulations in the law as a fundamental remedy," and "According to the proposal submitted by the Fruit and Produce Trade Association, the organization of trade associations is originally intended to promote overall unity, enhance public interests, and correct abuses. Therefore, all members of the same trade, regardless of affiliation, should respect the law, join the association, and work together for common well-being. Without mandatory membership measures, those who have already joined bear all the obligations, such as raising funds for national and municipal bonds, providing disaster relief, and other obligations stipulated by law, while those who have not joined can remain uninvolved. As for the benefits and protections that the law should provide, there is no distinction between those who have joined and those who have not. Those who have joined feel bound by the law, association regulations, and resolutions, while those who have not joined have no such restrictions. Relatively speaking, those who have joined often find it more convenient to withdraw, and trade associations are on the verge of collapse. It is hoped that the general meeting will resolve to request the government to clearly stipulate that all members of the same trade should uniformly join the trade association to ensure unity," etc. It is noted that in recent years, the government has entrusted various associations with the responsibility of raising funds for the issuance of government bonds and treasury bills, but the authority of each association only extends to its members, making it difficult to handle affairs. This is especially true of voluntary membership, which greatly hinders the exercise of the association's powers. Other abuses have been detailed by the two associations and need not be repeated. Moreover, if the number of businesses in the same trade exceeds seven, they may not join the chamber of commerce as store members, as stipulated in Article 10 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law. The current law clearly stipulates that trade associations are compulsory organizations, not based on a laissez-faire approach. However, associations rely on their members for their existence. If associations are forcibly organized, but membership remains voluntary, the association will inevitably become a mere formality, which is inconsistent with the fundamental purpose of compulsory organization and seems contradictory. Based on the above reasons, it was resolved at the general meeting of the affiliated association on June 27th to request your ministry to supplement the Implementing Rules of the Trade Association Law with a provision requiring all members of the same trade to join the association. It is appropriate to record this case and submit a document for your review and action."

Guo Jingluan Reports on the Discovery of Martyr Cai's Remains 80

Guo Jingluan, the widow of Cai Gongshi, hosted the local press at Gongshi Middle School at 5 p.m. yesterday. More than twenty people attended. The following is Guo's report on the discovery of the remains of Martyr Cai Gongshi:

(1) Motivation for Investigating the Remains: After the martyrdom of Cai and others, Jingluan, after completing the funeral arrangements, immediately requested the government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to allow her to go to Jinan to investigate and retrieve the remains. At that time, Mr. Tan Yankai told her that the remains of the martyrs were said to be in the backyard of the Diplomatic Affairs Office and that they would have to wait until the Jinan Incident was resolved before they could be recovered. Mr. Wang Zhengting also advised her to wait a while and comforted her. Jingluan, grieving for the deceased and wanting to establish a permanent memorial, decided to found Gongshi School. With the support of party and state veterans, she went overseas to raise funds. After returning to China last year, she was eager to open the school, and the Jinan Incident remained unresolved, so the matter was temporarily suspended. In January of this year, the Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters exposed the unscrupulous merchant Zhang Shuheng for privately renting the old Diplomatic Affairs Office to the Japanese, and requested the Shandong government to recover the land. Jingluan believed that since the remains of the martyrs were buried in the

Page 10

backyard of the Office, and the Japanese had taken the house under an alias, it was clear that they were plotting to obliterate the traces of the May Third Massacre. Therefore, she immediately submitted a request to the Central Party Headquarters and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government, asking them to order the Shandong Provincial Government to recover the land, severely punish the unscrupulous merchant, and request to personally investigate. However, due to illness and the demands of school affairs, it was delayed until February before she was able to travel to Jinan.

(2) Overview of the Two Trips to Jinan: Upon arriving in Jinan, Jingluan visited various party and government agencies and received strong support from Chairman Han, Mr. He Siyuan, and various party, government, and public organizations. As a result, a preparatory committee for commemorating the May Third Martyrs was formed. Its main measures were: (1) establishing a martyrs' tomb at the old Diplomatic Affairs Office, (2) converting the house into a martyrs' shrine, (3) casting a bronze statue of Cai, and (4) founding the May Third School. Proper arrangements were also made for investigating and retrieving the remains, and preparations were made for excavation. At this time, Jingluan received telegrams from Beijing and Shanghai reporting that overseas donors who had contributed to the construction of the school building had sent representatives back to China to inspect the school site and needed to meet with Jingluan. Reluctantly, she had to return. After returning, she fell ill and was busy with the school's affairs. After the May Third Commemoration Meeting, she went to Jinan again. In addition to resolving to do her best to recover the house where the martyrs died and establish the bronze statue of the martyrs, the martyrs' shrine, and the May Third School, she also began excavating the remains. After arriving in Jinan and making contact, she rushed to Beiping to inquire about the situation of the Republic University, which was originally founded by Cai. Party and government agencies in Beiping held a public memorial service for Cai at Zhongshan Park in Beiping. At the same time, the conference telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to quickly resolve the May Third Massacre. Jingluan was anxious to excavate the remains of the martyrs and hurriedly returned to Jinan on June 21st.

(3) The Reality of the Excavation: After arriving in Jinan, she convened the fifth meeting of the preparatory committee for commemorating the May Third Martyrs on the 23rd and resolved to excavate on the 24th. On that day, Jingluan, along with the relatives of the martyrs Han Chun, Sun Wuxue, Rong and Cai's guards Shen Changsheng and other workers, went to the backyard of the old Diplomatic Affairs Office. The excavation site was in the southwest corner of the garden, which was originally a place where workers took soil. After digging more than two feet, only the mat and rope used to wrap the bodies on the day of the martyrdom were found, all of which had rotted, and no bones were found. Further down was hard soil, which was deeply disappointing. However, Jingluan was not reconciled and ordered the workers to search and dig nearby, but nothing was found. On the 25th, they continued to excavate in the southwest corner of the garden. All the loose soil in the backyard was dug up, and Japanese water bottles, military knives, stirrups, and belts were found in the middle of the ground, along with more than a dozen military uniforms. Although no bones were found, Jingluan reasoned that the bones must also be in the backyard and ordered the workers to continue searching. Until 5 p.m., the excavation was carried out in the southwest corner of the garden, about ten feet from the south wall and about fifteen feet from the west wall. Only five inches into the ground, the burnt bones of the martyrs, cremated by the Japanese, were found. All that was seen was bone ash, skulls, limb bones, pelvic bones, rib bones, finger bones, and the remains of burnt military Shandong maps, shoe soles, clothes, belts, etc. The scene was heartbreaking and unbearable. She could only cry loudly to vent her grief. Then she used paper bags to collect them one by one and placed them in ceramic basins. She immediately reported to reporters from various newspapers at the Diplomatic Affairs Office and notified the preparatory committee for commemorating the May Third Martyrs. She visited Chairman Han and Mr. He Siyuan, and telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government in Jingluan's personal name. On the 26th, she continued to excavate and collect, and the Shandong government still had no appropriate measures to take. The preparatory committee for commemorating the May Third Martyrs advocated putting them in ceramic urns and burying them temporarily. Jingluan believed that this was inappropriate and feared accidents. Jingluan personally visited the chairman, who had approved bringing them back. She decided to collect the ashes in a box and carry them to Beijing, departing from Pupu south in the morning of the 27th.

(4) Japanese Consul Nishida's Shock: Nishida, the Japanese consul stationed in Jinan, had been paying close attention to Jingluan's trip to Jinan, the investigation of the remains, and the resolutions after the establishment of the preparatory committee for commemorating the May Third Massacre. This time, Jingluan finally discovered the ashes of the martyrs who had been cremated by the Japanese in an attempt to obliterate the traces of the massacre. The Japanese in Jinan were very panicked, and Nishida was even more shocked. He had sent a detailed telegram to the Japanese government to report. However, Jingluan believed that the Japanese brutally murdered diplomatic officials and opened an unprecedented international precedent, causing the May Third Massacre. This hatred and shame will never be forgotten by the Chinese people. For the rest of their lives, they vow to avenge it. Even any country or people in the world who uphold humanity and justice have recognized their barbarous hearts. No matter how cleverly the Japanese try to conceal it with deceitful propaganda, how can they easily cover up the facts? Although these bones were cremated, they were finally discovered. Our people have a greater understanding of their brutal face and insidious methods, and it is enough to prove that the Japanese are indeed a ironclad proof of harming our country's diplomatic officials in our country's diplomatic missions. In future negotiations on the Jinan Incident, this will naturally be the prerequisite. At the same time, I hope that countries that uphold humanitarianism and justice will also give our country sympathetic assistance, so that in the future, the world's international relations will not be caused by this inhuman Japanese who create the evil precedent of harming diplomatic officials. Therefore, our people believe that the Japanese Consul Nishida's shock and report this time shows that the Japanese are trying to cover up their crimes, which is futile and will only cause deeper resentment at recent wounds.

(5) Request for the Arrangement of the Remains: Jingluan originally intended to send the remains to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for review. When she arrived in Beijing, she was exhausted from crying too much. The Foreign Minister Wang had already arrived in Shanghai, and the next day was Monday's memorial week, so she did not meet with the authorities and did not draft a written report. Therefore, she returned to the bureau to rest. Now, in addition to telegraphing Chairman Chiang to ask for instructions, she has also submitted requests to the Central Party Headquarters, the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, including: 1. Appealing to the National Government to mourn the martyrs' sacrifice for the country and order a state funeral. 2. Appealing to the National Government to send personnel to receive the remains of the martyrs, report the process, invite them to Beijing to identify the bones, and serve the spirits together. In addition, she has telegraphed the country to report the details, and will also make appropriate requests to our country's diplomatic authorities. She will also appeal to all countries in the world to uphold justice.

Trial of Injured Employees in the Domestic Goods Department Store Case Today 81

Chinese Directors and Committee Members to Meet Tomorrow

The trial of the injured employees in the Domestic Goods Department Store case will be held today. The Chinese directors and committee members of the Shanghai Municipal Council will hold a discussion meeting tomorrow to discuss everything. Employees, workers and merchants all held a general meeting yesterday. The situation yesterday is recorded below,

Employee General Meeting: The Federation of Employees of the Domestic Goods Department Store held a general meeting at 3 p.m. yesterday to discuss the aftermath and all issues related to employees and workers. More than 600 people attended. Chen Weixin was elected as chairman and reported on the progress of the negotiations. It was resolved that, in order to facilitate collective negotiation, seven committee members would be elected to take charge of the process. Dong Juesun, Chen Weixin, and others were elected as committee members. The meeting adjourned at 7 p.m.

Merchant General Meeting: The Federation of Merchants held a representative general meeting at 2 p.m. yesterday. Liu Zhongying chaired the meeting and reported on the purpose of the meeting. It was resolved that: 1. Letters would be sent to the Chinese directors and organizations to pay attention to the losses suffered by the merchants, and letters would also be sent to the Chinese directors and mediators that the association would send people to listen in on the meeting at Yipinxian on the 7th of this month. 2. It was resolved to hire legal counsel. 3. All expenses will be borne by the members. 4. A banquet will be held for the Chinese directors, organizations, mediators, and reporters.

Letter to Chinese Directors: The Federation of Merchants sent a letter to the Chinese directors yesterday, stating: "Dear Sirs, We read in the newspaper that you will be convening a meeting of the negotiation committee of the Domestic Goods Department Store case and relevant personnel at Yipinxian on the afternoon of the 7th to discuss the department store case. Before this discussion, the losses suffered by our merchants should be communicated to you for handling. Since the occurrence of this case, the losses suffered by our merchants have been the most significant. The facts and details have been communicated in previous letters, and we hope you are aware of them. A list of the verified losses is attached for your review. We sincerely request that you raise this for discussion when attending the meeting, and we hope you will pay special attention to these losses."

Bonus and Housing Issues for Employees of China General Edison Company 82

Social Bureau to Mediate Today

Due to the insincerity of the company in resolving the issues of treatment and conditions, the electrical workers of China General Edison Company implemented a policy of allowing passengers to ride the streetcars without buying tickets. After persuasion by the Social Bureau, they resumed work at 5 p.m. the day before yesterday. The bureau has scheduled mediation today. The situation is recorded below.

Resumption of Work: At 5 p.m. the night before last, the union sent traffic teams to various locations to order ticket sellers to resume work and issued a public notice. By 5:30 p.m., all ticket sellers on routes 1, 2, 3, and 4 resumed selling tickets as usual. The union has scheduled to send Zhou Guangrong, Zhu Hanhe, and three other representatives to the company again at 10 a.m. today to inquire when the general manager will implement the nine signed agreements, when the members of the welfare committee will be appointed, when medical matters will be discussed, when workers' life insurance will be implemented, and when the amount of retirement pay before the end of May 20 will be settled.

Union Statement: A reporter from the New Voice News met with the executive director of the union yesterday. According to him, the members of the union have been unable to make ends meet due to soaring prices, so on March 25, the general meeting passed a resolution to improve treatment. However, the company showed no sincerity. After repeated mediation by the Social Bureau, the Public Security Bureau, and the Municipal Party Department, nine conditions were signed on May 28, stipulating that they would be implemented from June 1. The issues of workers' bonuses and housing were to be negotiated separately. Until now, the nine conditions have not been implemented. The union has repeatedly negotiated unsuccessfully. The day before yesterday, the representative general meeting resolved to implement a policy of allowing passengers to ride the streetcars without buying tickets to promote awareness. After receiving the instructions from the Social Bureau, the union sent representatives to inquire with the company. The company made various excuses and gave no concrete answers. After repeated persuasion by Xu Zhi of the Social Bureau, in order to obey the orders of the higher authorities, they immediately resumed work at 5 p.m. If the company is still insincere in today's mediation, the second warning will be given.

Mediation Today: In order to quickly resolve the China General Edison Company workers' strike, the Municipal Social Bureau, in addition to ordering the company to fulfill the nine conditions that have been agreed and signed by both labor and management, immediately sent personnel to persuade the workers to resume work and wait for mediation. It has scheduled a mediation committee meeting at 2 p.m. today and invited the Municipal Party Department and the Public Security Bureau to send committee members to participate in the mediation of workers' housing and bonus issues. The first district water and electricity workers' union has appointed Zhu Hanhe and Zhou Guangrong as responsible representatives to attend and await mediation.

Points of Contention: The most intense disputes between labor and management at China General Edison Company that cannot be resolved are the two issues of workers' bonuses and housing. The original proposal and reasons put forward by the labor side are as follows: (1) (Housing) The company allocates 200,000 yuan to purchase land and build workers' housing, limited to completion by the end of the 20th year. Before completion, the company will pay a housing subsidy of 10 yuan per person per month. After completion, if there is not enough space to live in, the workers who do not live in the workers' housing will still be given a housing subsidy. The workers' housing is the property of the company and rented to workers for living. The rent is calculated at 6% weekly interest on the total cost of land purchase and construction. However, the rent for public housing in the workers' housing (such as schools for workers' children and cooperative societies) will be borne by the company. Reason: Workers' housing was stipulated in the 16th year treaty to be built by the company on land it found, but it has been four years and it has not yet been implemented, which is a pity. Therefore, it is specifically limited to completion before the end of the 20th year, and the company is requested to bear the housing subsidy before completion. Workers are not construction experts, and the so-called 200,000 is a hypothetical number. If there is not enough space in the completed housing, the company should still bear the housing subsidy. The completed housing will still be the property of the company and rent will be collected. In the 17th and 18th years, the total amount of the company's loans and bank transactions was more than 500,000 yuan. The company also earns interest by depositing money in the bank. Building workers' housing also earns interest, which does not cause the company any losses. However, the company's interest rate for workers should not be too high, so we request that the rent be calculated at 6% weekly interest. This housing is not only cheaper to rent, but because workers live together, it is easier to run labor businesses such as consumer cooperatives, which can reduce workers' living expenses other than rent. It is estimated that each worker's family living in workers' housing can save 10 yuan per month. Therefore, before and after completion, if they do not live in the workers' housing, the company should pay a housing subsidy of 10 yuan per person per month. (2) Bonuses: From the 20th year onwards, the board of directors will be responsible for submitting a proposal to the shareholders' meeting for the distribution of workers' bonuses. No less than 96% of the net profit each year will be allocated, of which 60% will be used as a fund for labor undertakings, and 40% will be distributed to workers according to the size of their wages. Those who have been reprimanded three times or given a major demerit once in a year will have their share of the surplus reduced by half. Those who have been reprimanded six times or given a major demerit twice will not be given their share of the surplus. The surplus that is reduced or not given will be used to fund labor undertakings. Reason: According to Article 55 of the revised company charter in the 18th year, Article 5 of the 16th year, and the previous treaty, 3/15 is equal to 4.2% of the company charter. According to the previous treaty, workers get 60% of 3/15, which is 3/25, and staff get 40% of 3/15, which is 2/25. According to the company charter, shareholders get 16.8% of the 21%, which is 20/25. So the proportion of surplus is three to two for workers and staff, and three to twenty for workers and shareholders. The ratio of the number of workers to staff is five to one. Why is the proportion of surplus three to two? Why is the surplus divided among shareholders four times that of staff and workers? We cannot understand it after much thought. But the result is very clear: those with money get more, and the rich get richer. Those without capital who sell their labor get less, and the poor are always poor. Sun Yat-sen said, "The purpose of our Kuomintang's livelihood principle is to equalize the wealth in society." He also said, "Prevent the big problem of unequal wealth in the future society." The current method of distributing surplus is one of the causes of this big problem. When promoting party ideology under the blue sky and white sun, this cause of disease cannot be allowed to exist. The original elements of running a company are capital and labor. The size of the rewards should be determined by the level of efficiency. The reward for capital is dividends, and the reward for labor is wages. Logically, rewards can represent the level of efficiency, but the current facts are not necessarily so. However, it is undeniable that the only ones who suffer are the workers who sell their labor. Now we painfully admit that the current reward can represent the level of efficiency. Then, at a minimum, the distribution of surplus should also be determined according to the current reward. According to the company's business report for the 18th year, the salaries of staff were 125,000 yuan, the capital dividend was 240,000 yuan, and the workers' wages were 339,000 yuan (disregarding the remainder). The proportion of the three rewards is: staff is 1 (actual 1.92), capital is 2, and workers is 3 (actual 2.73). That is, workers should get half of the total surplus, or at least acknowledge 1% of the 21% stipulated in the company's charter as the interest of preferred shares, and 8% as the interest of the founders' red shares. There is still 19.2% left. Workers should get at least half of this 19.2%. Therefore, we demand that workers should not get less than 96% of the 21% in the surplus. We should follow Sun Yat-sen's instructions and use the surplus we get to "improve the lives of laborers." We will use 60% as a fund for labor undertakings to run labor businesses to improve the lives of members. This is the most cost-effective way. At the same time, we will take into account the special circumstances of each member and distribute the remaining part to each member for their own disposal. Reducing and not giving surplus due to mistakes is in accordance with the provisions of Article 40 of the Factory Law. As for the surplus that is reduced or not given, it is not a benefit that the company should get, so please allocate it to the funds for labor undertakings.

Heavy Rain Slightly Relieves the Sweltering Heat 84

Low-lying Areas Accumulate Water into Puddles

Dog Electrocuted on Zhijiang Road

Since the beginning of summer in this city, the humid heat has been scorching, making it difficult to bear. The thermometer often rises to around ninety degrees. This kind of weather is happening even before the hottest period, and people say that this year will be bitterly hot, which is probably not an exaggeration. After the sweltering heat, people are eagerly hoping for thunderstorms; almost everyone feels the same way. Yesterday morning, there was heavy rain, and it cleared up at noon. Then, at about 5:15 PM, there was thunder and lightning again, and heavy rain poured down. The continuous heat was slightly relieved, and the farmers in the surrounding rural areas had just finished transplanting rice seedlings, so this timely rain was also very beneficial.

Torrential Rain: Yesterday morning's heavy rain suddenly cleared up towards noon, and the scorching sun was high in the sky, making it as sweltering as before. It wasn't until 5:10 PM that dark clouds gathered, and it suddenly became gloomy. The heavy rain began to fall from the end of the sky and continued, refreshing people's spirits. In an instant, thunder rumbled, lightning flashed, and the torrential rain poured down. Pedestrians disappeared from the roads, and every household closed their windows and doors. The heavy rain lasted for about half an hour, and then people disappeared from the roads, and every household closed their windows and doors. The heavy rain lasted for about half an hour before it stopped. Several more showers fell in the evening, but they were not as heavy.

Glimpse of the Roads: During the heavy rain, trams and buses generally stopped running. In Zhabei, along Baoshan Road, Taiyangmiao Road, and Chang'an Road, the water was knee-deep in places. In the public concession, near North Zhejiang Road and Sanmalu Tianchan Theater, and at Daxin Street, Racecourse, etc., the water accumulated in the roads to a depth of more than a foot due to the inability of the sewers to drain it. Pedestrians all hired rickshaws to cross, so rickshaw pullers had a prosperous business, earning several times their usual income. In the French concession, along East and West Zilaihuo Streets, Dongjie Bridge Street, Songshan Road, and Baxianqiao, the water was also several inches deep, creating a vast expanse of water. Cars splashed water everywhere, and many pedestrians had their clothes soiled. The Suzhou River suddenly swelled, rising by more than a foot.

Everything Turned into a Swamp: Low-lying areas were ankle-deep in water after the rain, turning everything into a swamp. Many of the shacks built by Jiangbei migrants along Xiaoshadu Road and Roberts Road in Western Shanghai, as well as the Taiyangmiao and Suzhou River banks in Zhabei, were washed away by the rain. The lowest-lying areas were more than a foot deep in water, and the water did not recede all night.

Lights Extinguished: During the heavy rain, the lights suddenly went out in the Datong Road and Nanxing Road areas of Zhabei. It was found that the power lines had been broken by the rain. However, the lights were restored to their original state shortly after. It was also heard that a wild mulberry tree on Zhijiang Temple Road was struck by lightning and fell, and a yellow dog was electrocuted to death.

Fierce Battle in Ladu Road to Capture Thieves 85

One Thief Killed, Four Thieves Escaped

Both the Vietnamese Constable and Western Detective Were Injured

Yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM, a dye shop on Ladu Road in the French Concession was robbed. At the time, a Western detective, a Vietnamese constable, and a patrolman happened to be passing by. The two sides exchanged gunfire. As a result, one thief was killed, and the Western detective and Vietnamese constable were seriously injured. The details are recorded below.

Five Thieves Suddenly Arrive at the Dye Shop: The dye and weaving factory at 393-6 Ladu Road in the French Concession, owned by a Zhang family and named Jinhua, had a relatively prosperous business. Unexpectedly, it attracted the attention of thieves. Yesterday afternoon around 3:00 PM, five thieves suddenly arrived, each wearing different styles of clothing. Two thieves were armed with pistols. After entering the shop, they first drove all the shop assistants and servants into one room and then divided up to search as they pleased.

Shop Assistant Secretly Follows the Thieves: The thieves searched the room thoroughly, but apart from various silks, there was nothing of value. The thieves discarded these easily identifiable stolen goods and only snatched a gold ring from an employee's hand before leaving the shop in frustration. At that time, a shop assistant named Jia, who was very alert, secretly followed the thieves, waiting for an opportunity to act.

Thieves and Constables Shot: After leaving the shop, the thieves fled north. Jia followed closely behind, tailing them to near Ladu Road and Avenue Joffre. Not far from the factory, about 300 yards away, Vietnamese Constable Jia, number 112, was standing there. Jia secretly informed the constable, who quickly drew his gun and fired at the thieves. One thief fell in response, and the remaining thieves returned fire wildly. The constable was hit in the waist by a bullet and immediately fell to the ground in pain.

Western Detective Injured in Both Feet: During the exchange of gunfire, Western Detective Mamlone from the special agency political department of the French Police Department happened to be returning to his residence at 97 Ladu Road by car. He saw the Vietnamese constable fall to the ground and, without regard for danger, jumped out of the car with his gun and exchanged fire with the thieves. As a result, the detective was shot twice in the foot, and a stray bullet injured a Russian man riding in a rickshaw. The police department heard the alarm and immediately dispatched detectives to search and arrest the thieves. The four thieves had already disappeared without a trace. A pistol was found near the injured thief. The injured people and the thief were taken to the hospital for treatment in separate vehicles.

Injured Thief Died After Unsuccessful Treatment: The injured thief was taken to Guangci Hospital, where he died after unsuccessful treatment due to the severity of his injuries. The hospital notified the police department, which sent detectives to transport the thief's body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch mortuary for an autopsy. The thief was wearing a white undershirt, Xiangyun gauze pants, and a toupee with a flat top. He was wearing gray silk stockings and iron machine flower satin shoes. The bullet entered from the left breast near the front of the chest and grazed between the left and right eyebrows. It is said that the Vietnamese constable's injuries are also severe.

Heartless Female Waitress 86

Lovesick Man Commits Suicide by Poisoning

Wei Fuyuan from Pudong, 28 years old, was formerly the manager of Huaxingcheng Board Box Store at New Garbage Bridge. Recently, he resigned on July 1 due to disagreements with the store owner. He immediately took his luggage to Huashang Villa on Haining Road and temporarily resided in room 34. Yesterday morning at 3:30 AM, he suddenly secretly swallowed a large dose of lifeproducing smoke poison to commit suicide. Later, the waiter discovered it and urgently reported it to the accounting room, which in turn reported it to the Huishi police station. Officer 601 was ordered to come and send him to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He died at 1:30 PM in the afternoon. His body was immediately transported to the mortuary for an autopsy, pending a report to the court for an examination. It is said that three years ago, Wei opened a Wei Hecheng Board Box Shop in Xingye Li on North Shanxi Road. He often went to the Tianyun Building of Yong'an Company to hang out, where he met a female waitress from Songjiang named Zhu Pin Fang. They were deeply in love, feeling like they had met each other too late. Over time, they began to cohabitate, and he gave Zhu Pin Fang 20 yuan a month. However, fate was fickle, and the store's business suffered too much losses. By January of this year, it was unsustainable and eventually closed down. Zhu, seeing this unfavorable situation, fled without a trace. At this time, Wei suffered this misfortune and was extremely depressed, like someone drunk or crazy, for about ten days. Later, through the recommendation of colleagues, he was hired at Huaxingcheng Store. However, he never forgot about Zhu Pin Fang. When he had free time, he went to the North Railway Station area to search for her. The day before yesterday (the 3rd), he met Zhu on the road, and they went to Huashang Villa for a night of secrecy. Yesterday morning, Zhu suddenly made an excuse to go out, saying that she would return in a moment. Wei believed it to be true and had no doubts. Until midnight, she had not returned. For a moment, overwhelmed by anger, he suddenly had the thought of death and committed suicide by poisoning. It is also very pitiful.

Banning Cars Racing for Pleasure 87

Chief Chen of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued proclamation Zheng Zi No. 14 yesterday, which reads: "Regarding the matter of issuing a proclamation, it is noted that racing cars and horses is already prohibited. Recently, with the arrival of the hot summer, many residents of this city are taking cars out for pleasure, even increasing their speed and overtaking at will, resulting in frequent accidents. This bureau's duty is to strictly prohibit this behavior in order to prevent danger. In addition to ordering the chiefs of each district to instruct the police to investigate and prohibit this behavior at all times, it is hereby proclaimed for everyone to be aware. In the future, if it is found that any car is racing for pleasure or increasing its speed to overtake, it will be punished and no leniency will be given. This is a crucial proclamation."

Issue with Liquor Industry Permit Occurs 90

Public Monopoly Bureau Representative Provides No Definite Response

Will Petition Various Agencies for Relief

The Shanghai Liang Liquor Industry Association convened an emergency meeting of all members at 2:00 PM yesterday because the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau failed to issue liquor storage permits in accordance with regulations. More than 30 members of the association attended. Zhou Chaozhang and Fang Qinbo, representatives from the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau, and He Xiangsheng, chairman, attended the meeting. The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, stating that it had been four days since the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau opened, and the bureau had failed to issue liquor storage permits to the various businesses in accordance with regulations. Today, representatives from the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau are attending the association's general meeting and should provide an explanation to dispel the members' doubts. Zhou Chaozhang, a representative from the Bureau, spoke, stating that the reason the bureau had not issued the liquor storage permits to the various businesses was that the former Second District Bai Liquor Public Monopoly Tax Collection Office had not completed the transfer, so there was no basis for issuing the permits. Zhang Guanshou, Zhu Qingtang, and He Xiangsheng then spoke one after another, stating that the Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau and the Second District Bai Liquor Public Monopoly Tax Collection Office were both state taxation agencies, and the public fees paid by merchants to the Second District Bai Liquor Public Monopoly Tax Collection Office were naturally valid. There was no reason for the state agency to interrupt the service. Since one side has already opened, the other side must have already completed the transfer. The Bureau's failure to issue the liquor storage permits in violation of regulations has caused the merchants to suspend business and suffer great losses. Fang Qinbo, a representative from the Bureau, then spoke, stating that the Bureau should urge the former office to complete the transfer in order to have a basis for issuing the liquor storage permits. He Xiangsheng and Zhu Qingtang replied that the transfer issue was the responsibility of the Bureau and the former office and that the merchants had no right to interfere. Furthermore, the merchants did not know when the Tax Collection Office would complete the transfer. They requested that the Bureau immediately send people to investigate the inventory of each business and issue the liquor storage permits. Otherwise, the merchants would suspend business, resulting in great losses, and would have to publish a statement in the newspaper and petition for relief. At this point, the Bureau representatives announced their withdrawal, and the discussion began: (1) The Shangbao Tobacco and Alcohol Public Monopoly Bureau has not issued liquor inventory permits, and the Bureau's representatives have not provided a definite response for a long time, hindering business and violating regulations. How should this be handled? Resolution: A. Petition the National Government, the Ministry of Finance, and the Provincial Bureau for relief. B. Send a letter to the Bureau to negotiate. C. Publish a statement in the newspaper based on regulations, explaining the association's position. (2) The newspaper reported that the Fuji Distillery, etc., had recorded the number of Yellow Liquor Public Monopoly prices, fearing that there would still be floating prices in the future. Should the association express its opinion? Resolution: Publish a statement in the newspaper, stating that if there are any changes to the regulations, the association will firmly oppose them. (3) Xu Qingrong, a representative from Tongdeyong Liquor Store, sent a letter stating that he would transfer the brand name to Li Guangzhen and add Huiji and requested registration. Resolution: If the store pays the overdue fees in full, it will be registered. The meeting was adjourned after the discussions.

In Jungong Road, Jiansong Bridge

Witness Testimony Unfavorable to Abao

The Court Will Investigate the Guarantor

Since the disappearance of Ni Guangxun, a student at Great China University, last winter, Fan Abao, who claims to be Ni's wife, suddenly filed a lawsuit with the civil court of the Special District Court against Ni's sister, Zeng Ni Liujie, accusing her of encroaching on the family property and refusing to return it. The case has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper after several summons. The Special Court summoned the defendant, Zeng Ni Liujie, again the other day, and she was still represented by her lawyer, Zhang Deqin. The plaintiff, Fan Abao, first stated that today's witness, Ni Wenming, has arrived in court and is fully aware of all the facts of the case. Please question him. As for the deposit, it did exist, but Guangxun had used it all up when he was studying in Shanghai, leaving only forty taels. There is a bank passbook to prove this. As for the claim that Guangxun voluntarily gave Fan two thousand taels, it cannot be deeply believed based solely on empty words. The plaintiff's request to demand the return of the property from the defendant based on what kind of status is a fundamental error and an extravagant desire. It should be rejected. The interrogator stated that although the plaintiff's request for litigation relief in this case had been approved, the guarantor provided had not been clearly investigated and announced a postponement of the hearing.

Mauser Gun Belonged to a Dutchman

Investigation Reveals Theft by Two Resigned Servants

Feng Baishun, a Chinese detective from the Huishi Police Department, along with detectives Shang Wu and Xizhu, received a report from informants the other morning that a gang of thieves was conspiring in a restaurant at 717 Zhejiang Road, with the intention of committing illegal acts. leather suitcase. They then went to 634 Dagu Road and arrested Xue Baoquan and his mistress, Xue Yan. A total of eleven men and women were arrested one after another and taken back to the police station. The other morning, they were sent to the Second Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, stepped forward to state the previous events and claimed that the defendants had used weapons to rob property at 49 Fujian Road. As for the Mauser gun that was seized, it has also been confirmed that the gun came from a Dutchman named Lamboo, who lived at 250 Hongqiao Road. In March of this year, Lamboo carried the gun to the工部局 to obtain a license and then left Shanghai. His wife also went to the hospital for treatment in April or May, so she locked the pistol in the cabinet. Until yesterday, when the Chinese and Western detectives went to investigate, the Western woman did not know that the gun had been stolen. The key was not damaged, and there were no signs of forced entry on the cabinet. It is suspected that it was done by two of the Western woman's servants, who resigned in May while the Western woman was in the hospital. Therefore, they are highly suspicious of these two people. They requested a postponement to investigate further. He then presented the pistol as evidence. After interrogating each of the defendants, Judge Wu Tingqi ordered a postponement of the hearing to July 13. The defendants were returned to custody separately.

Doctor and Scribe's Extortion Letter Scam 95

Zhai Miaogen's Confession Seems Convincing

Jiang Xiyuan Still Claims Slander

Jiang Weibin, a local resident and owner of the slaughterhouse located at 16 Fengtian Road, received multiple threatening letters from gangsters between July of last year and June 28th of this year, totaling seven letters. Initially, they demanded 2,000 yuan, later reduced to 1,200 yuan. They also arranged a meeting near the Longwang Temple in the Nanhui County area of Pudong. Jiang reported this to the police, who dispatched detectives and apprehended three suspects: Jiang Xiyuan (also known as Xiguang), Qian Zhensen, and Zhai Miaogen, all from Pudong. They were handed over to the Special District Local Court for interrogation and detention.

The previous morning, Judge Xiao Xieufen held a further trial. The police lawyer stated that the defendant Zhai Miaogen had confessed to writing the threatening letters at the police station. After investigation, it was found that Qian Zhensen was not involved in the case and should be released. Zhai Miaogen, questioned as a doctor, confessed that he knew Jiang Xiguang and was asked to write two letters to Jiang Weibin demanding 2,000 yuan. Because he was related to Jiang, it was inconvenient for him to write the letters himself. The meeting place was inside the Xiaoshijie Amusement Park in the city. However, Jiang had a headache and couldn't go at the last minute, so he asked me to go. At the time, I was hesitant and consulted a fortune teller who said there was no sign of wealth, so I didn't go to the negotiation. In June of last year, Jiang came again, saying that the previous two letters had demanded too much, and now he wanted to reduce the demand to 1,200 yuan, which would be effective. So I wrote several more letters based on his drafts. Recently, Jiang came and said that Jiang Lao Ban had introduced business and still planned to proceed with the extortion, asking me to write a letter to arrange a meeting at the Dajing Class in Sincere Company.

When questioned, Jiang Xiguang claimed that Zhai Miaogen's confession was entirely fabricated and was a malicious slander. He asked for a clear judgment. Judge Xiao reviewed the confessions and ordered Qian Zhenmiao to provide a guarantee to be available for summons at any time. Jiang and Zhai were returned to custody, and the trial was adjourned.

Bandits Emerging from Cemetery Hills 96

Vegetable Vendors Greatly Frightened

Three Bandits and Stolen Goods Recovered

Yesterday at 2:00 AM, a vegetable vendor, Mr. Jia, was carrying vegetables past Chenjiamen near the eastern end of Qichang Wharf in Pudong. Suddenly, three bandits emerged from the cemetery hills, brandishing pistols and threatening him to remain silent. They robbed him of one silver dollar and eighteen dimes. The members of the third squad of the local defense corps learned of the incident and divided up to encircle and capture the bandits. They apprehended two bandits south of Chenjia, and recovered a fake pistol, an iron chisel, and the original stolen money of one dollar and eight dimes from them.

Under interrogation, they confessed. One, Xia Baozi, 32 years old, from Dongtai, lived in Caonitang, Yangjiadu, and worked as a dock coolie. The other, Shi Songmingshan, 25 years old, from Suqian, lived with Xia. Both bandits admitted that they were driven by poverty to rob passersby. They also revealed the name of their accomplice, Cai Zhanxian, who was hiding at 1 Xintongtang, Yangjiadu. Captain Xu sent the original squad members to arrest Cai and brought him back to the team. A single-edged sword and a flashlight were found in Cai's home. Yesterday, the witnesses were handed over to the corps headquarters and then transferred to the Third District Public Security Bureau for forwarding to the General Bureau for interrogation.

Young Girl Comes to Shanghai to Find Father, Nearly Abducted 97

Zhou Bingsheng's Bad Intentions

Cao Jinhua, a girl of fourteen years old, lived in Taishang, outside the South Gate of Changshu. Her father, Cao Sheng, worked as a carpenter at 23 Panxiang Alley, Sanpailou, in Shanghai. The day before, Jinhua was sent to Shanghai by her mother to visit her father on a steamboat. However, after arriving at the Xinzha Wharf yesterday morning, Zhou Bingsheng, a fellow passenger from Changshu, falsely claimed to know her father and offered to take her there. He lured her to the North Station, bought a Wusong train ticket, and boarded the train with her. Jinhua, who had never taken a train to her father's place before, became frightened and jumped off the train, crying out. The patrol police inquired about the situation, arrested Zhou, and sent him to the police station for transfer to the local court for interrogation.

The number of Dongtai natives in Shanghai has increased to tens of thousands. Starting from January of this year, a reunion has been organized, held on the first Sunday of each month, to exchange knowledge and connect with fellow townsmen. Li Baosheng, Qian Shusheng, Ge Gongzhen, Shi Bohang, and Lu Yuheng were elected as members of the preparation committee. Yesterday, a July luncheon was held at the YMCA assembly hall. The Ongoing Strike of French Municipal Council Workers 99

Du Yuesheng's Opinion

All the staff and workers of the French Municipal Council held an emergency general meeting yesterday, attended by over four thousand people. Liu Zhigang was publicly elected as the interim chairman, and Wang Zhuangyong and Gu Xigeng were the recorders. After the formalities, the chairman reported on the negotiations of the previous day and proposed important motions:

(1) Motion on the formation of working groups by committee members: Resolved, divided into document, communication, accounting, and general affairs departments. The document department nominated Gao Pengcheng, Wang Zhuangyong, Gao Zhenchang, Qiu Gaogang, Dong Shu, Gu Xigeng, Xie Xuefang, and Wang Binghui. The communication department nominated Yang Wugang, Tang Liang, Zhao Ziyun, Gao Songnian, Hu Fangdian, Liu Zhigang, Shen Guanlin, and Shen Caigeng. The accounting department nominated Ding Youzhi and Wei Shanxin. The general affairs department nominated Yang Wentao, Peng Quanfu, Tao Qipeng, Shen Sanhai, Zhou Qinren, Pan Wenqing, Wang Yaogen, Li Dinghai, Zhou Baisheng, and Yao Asan. Li Xiangchu and Wang Linbao were nominated as supplementary members.

(2) Motion on the election of five members of the temporary condition review committee: Resolved, Xie Xuefang, Gao Zhenchang, Liu Zhigang, Qiu Gaogang, and Gao Pengcheng were publicly elected.

(3) Motion on the publication of a strike publicity statement: Resolved, to be handled by the document department.

(4) Motion on the acceptance of requests from various public service agencies to participate: Resolved, to be handed over to the document department for publication in the newspapers.

(5) Motion on requesting assistance from the Chinese and French authorities: Resolved, to nominate Shen Guanlin to contact the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yang Wugang to contact the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Zhao Ziyun to contact the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, and Hu Fangdian, Gao Zhenchang, and Pan Wenqing to contact the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association.

(6) Motion on the surveillance of committee member Zhao Ziyun's actions by senior officials: Resolved, to request the Chief Engineer to issue a letter requesting his release.

(7) Motion on the use of the remaining funds and equipment from the former French Municipal Council Workers Union as temporary expenses for the current union: Resolved, to nominate Peng Quanfu to investigate the remaining funds and Shen Sanhai to investigate the equipment, etc.

(8) Motion on how to deal with the Municipal Council secretly sending people to sweep garbage, disrupting discipline during the strike: Resolved, the chief inspector shall dispatch a picket team to inspect in shifts day and night, with each shift serving six hours, and each shift consisting of five people, electing one leader to report to the union at any time in a free car for day and night rotation.

(9) Motion to propose that committee members take turns working at the union office: Resolved, approved. Each group will have two temporary committee members and four representatives working in shifts at night.

(10) Motion to propose requesting the labor-management contracts signed by the British Municipal Council and the French Water and Electricity Company for reference: Resolved, to send personnel to obtain them.

Due to wage issues, a strike occurred by the employees of the French Concession Municipal Council, and they requested the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers Association to uphold justice and provide assistance. In addition to replying to the employees' committee, the association stated that the garbage piled up on the road has been accumulating for several days, and with the continuous rainy weather, the foul odor is pervasive. If it is not cleaned up urgently, it will greatly affect the health of the residents. Therefore, a special letter was sent to Mr. Du Yuesheng, a Chinese director, to mediate. Yesterday afternoon, the employee representatives contacted Mr. Du, who strongly advised them to first clear the garbage piled up on the road to ensure public health, and then raise other conditions. The employee representatives respected Mr. Du's proposal and promised to continue working as usual on the road cleaning part.

Tax Exemption for Charitable Organizations' Houses 103

Reply from the Municipal Finance Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau had issued a notice to the Municipal South Inspection Office to collect property tax on all houses belonging to charitable organizations. Subsequently, the United Association of Charitable Organizations sent a letter to the bureau requesting exemption from the property tax payable by the owners. After several consultations, half a year has passed. Only yesterday did the charitable organizations receive a reply from the Finance Bureau, No. 595, stating, "The submitted applications have been noted. This case has been reported to the Municipal Government for approval, and it will continue to follow Article 15 of the Shanghai Property Tax Collection Rules, allowing charitable organizations to be exempt from property tax for the portion owned by the owners. Please be informed of this reply." It is said that all property taxes already collected from landlords will be refunded.

Tragic News of Natural Disasters and Banditry in Henan 106

The Chinese Red Cross Society recently received a telegram from the Nanwan branch requesting urgent relief, stating: The fierce bandit Cui Erdan attacked and occupied Tang County for seventeen days. Fortunately, Brigadier General Han Wenying of the 75th Division led his troops to recapture the city gates after a day of fighting. The people in the surrounding villages have lost everything – food, clothing, and shelter – and many have been brutally murdered. Our relief team has gone to Tang to provide assistance. Please forward a telegram to the National Government requesting urgent large-scale relief to save the survivors. Yao Shiyi of the Nanwan branch respectfully reports.

The Chinese Red Cross Society also received a telegram from Chairman Zhang of the Henan Provincial Relief Commission, stating: To the Chinese Red Cross Society: The disasters in Henan Province are escalating. Just when we hoped that the war would end and the people could rest, Heaven has brought down misfortune again. According to reports from Song County, Wen County, Wuyang County, Mianchi County, Lushi County, and other counties, starting from the date of the May Equinox, strong winds, torrential rain, and hailstones fell, with some as large as fists or eggs, and others shaped like beans or chestnuts. The disaster lasted for several hours, covering hundreds of miles. Unharvested wheat and newly grown crops were scorched and withered, and the destruction was almost complete. In several places, people and livestock were injured. The bandit Cui surrounded and attacked Nanyang, occupying the North Gate for several days, burning and looting Wen County with inhuman cruelty. He then led his troops to attack and capture Tanghe County, burning, killing, raping, and looting. More than two thousand people died, and over ten thousand were captured. Recently, they have been harassing Deng County, Nanzhao County, Tongbai County, and other places. The bandit army leaves villages and settlements in ruins, with fires burning brightly at night and killings rampant during the day. The disaster is even worse than the ravages of the Ming Dynasty bandit Li Zicheng. Daily reports of disasters are pouring in. Our commission has a responsibility to provide relief, but we lack the means. Therefore, we briefly describe the situation and urgently appeal to you to have compassion for the suffering people and provide large-scale relief. A drop of nectar can save countless lives, and millions of mourning people are awaiting your merciful protection. We eagerly await your reply. Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Provincial Relief Commission.

Nanjing Grand Theater Willing to Refund Ticket Prices 107

Due to Damage to Artificial Air Conditioning Machine

But Audience Loves Film and Doesn't Want to Leave

The night before last (Saturday), before 10:30 PM, the Nanjing Grand Theater announced that a small part of the installed air conditioning machine had suddenly broken down. The theater owner, unwilling for the audience to suffer from the heat, projected a slide stating that the artificial air conditioning machine was temporarily damaged and could not be started, and that the theater would gradually become hot. They offered to refund the ticket prices. At the time, the theater was showing the epic film "Secrets of Soviet Russia," which depicted Soviet Russia, and there were about a thousand audience members. Seeing the slide projected, they preferred to endure the heat rather than sacrifice the opportunity to watch this excellent film. Therefore, no one asked for a refund, and the theater immediately continued the screening. It is said that the air conditioning machine was repaired at 11:00 PM that night, so it was back to normal yesterday.

The Joint Firefighting Association was notified and informed the fire brigades in various districts, which immediately dispatched pump trucks to the scene to put out the fire with water. The fire was extinguished quickly, preventing further damage. Only a few items were burned.

The home of Xu Liansheng at No. 5 in Lane 796, Beile Road, French Concession, accidentally caught fire on the 20th of last month. The fire brigade rushed to extinguish it. Publication of "Accounting Supervision and Budget System" 111

Yin Gongwu's book "Accounting Supervision and Budget System" details modern fiscal thought and the development of auditing systems. It also provides a detailed comparative study of the accounting supervision systems of major countries around the world and concisely discusses the essence of the budget system. It includes a detailed discussion of the establishment of the Comptroller's Office and its scope of authority. The book is based on new materials and presents a thorough argument, making it a rare and up-to-date work that can serve as a good reference for China's fiscal policy. It is sold at the business department of the Shanghai Shandong Road Current Affairs News Agency, priced at five dimes per copy.

Draft Budget for Education Expenses in Jiangsu Province for the 20th Year (Shi Zhang) 116

The total amount of full collection and full expenditure is 4.88 million yuan.

16,552 yuan less than last year.

Time flies so fast. The 19th year has already ended, and the 20th year has come again. At this time last year, the reporter was collecting materials for "A Summary of the Budget for Education Expenses in Jiangsu Province in the 19th Year" (that article appeared in this newspaper on July 19, 20, and 21 of the 19th year). Now, the draft budget for education expenses in Jiangsu Province for the 20th year has been established. Jiangsu is the leading province, and its education expenses have long been independent, and the amount is larger than in other provinces, so many people are concerned about this matter. Now, based on what the reporter has heard and seen, the budget proposal for the 20th year will be described in detail below.

(1) The Process of Establishing the Budget 117

In early February this year, the Jiangsu Provincial Government issued a notice to all agencies in the province, requiring that all budget proposals for the 20th year be submitted to the Department of Finance for compilation by the end of February. According to the organizational principles of the Jiangsu Education Expense Committee, preparing the budget is one of the committee's responsibilities. Therefore, the committee held its 23rd meeting on February 27 at the Jiangsu Education Department in Zhenjiang. The committee members who attended were Ye Chucang, Chen Hexian, Wu Jingheng, Niu Yongjian, Chen Qicai, Zheng Yanghe, Liu Yizheng, Gao Yang, Wang Maozu, Ma Ketan, Gu Yuxiu, and eleven others. They discussed the budget issue for a full five hours - from 3:20 pm to 8:20 pm. As a result, only the revenue figures for provincial education in the 20th year were stipulated, totaling:

Land tax allocation: 2,500,000 yuan

Slaughter tax: 650,000 yuan

Brokerage tax: 650,000 yuan

(The above three items are the income of the Education Expense Management Office, totaling 3,800,000 yuan.)

Provincial treasury subsidy: 300,000 yuan

Tuition and lodging fees from various schools: 180,000 yuan

Outstanding funds allocated by the Ministry of Finance: 600,000 yuan

Total: 4,880,000 yuan

It was also resolved that the Education Department should compile an expenditure budget within this scope, taking into account the actual needs, and submit it to the meeting for discussion. This is the situation for determining the revenue.

After receiving the above resolution, the Education Department immediately began to compile the expenditure budget. However, the total revenue was less than last year, and on the expenditure side, not only could the original ones not be reduced, but in fact, many that had to be increased, such as the natural addition of grades in primary and secondary schools, the increase in teaching hours in junior high schools, the addition of vocational subjects in various middle schools, the addition of grades and equipment for rural teachers, the Jiangbei Farmers Education Center, the addition of grades in the Education College, and the natural development of social education institutions, etc., totaled 262,000 yuan, all of which were absolutely indispensable. Therefore, under these circumstances, the Education Department found it extremely difficult to consider adjustments and allocate funds. At the same time, it was also necessary to urge schools to compile and submit for review in advance. The exchange of official documents took quite a while. Therefore, it was not until the end of May that this part of the work was completed, taking almost three months.

The Education Department has received the "Draft Outline for the Distribution of Provincial Education Budget for the 20th Year" for drafting. The Education Expense Committee tentatively scheduled its 24th meeting for June 12. Just at that time, the Fourth Plenary Session of the Fifth Central Committee was being held, and members Ye and Wu were unable to come to the province, so it was rescheduled to the 23rd. The members who attended were almost the same as last time. It took four hours - from 3:35 pm to 7:40 pm - and finally the general amount of expenditures was resolved. Now, the general amounts of each item are listed below, and compared with the previous year:

Item Twentieth Year Amount Nineteenth Year Amount Comparison

1. Higher Education Expenses 1,339,152 yuan 1,399,152 yuan No increase or decrease

2. General Education Expenses 2,472,101 yuan 2,304,101 yuan Increase of 168,000 yuan

3. Social Education Expenses 630,587 increase 542,161 yuan Increase of 88,000 yuan

4. Study Abroad Expenses 175,000 yuan 172,000 yuan No increase or decrease

5. Other Agency Expenses 107,772 yuan 78,522 yuan Increase of 29,250 yuan

6. General Reserve Fund 95,388 yuan 397,190 increase Decrease of 301,82 yuan

Total 4,880,000 yuan 4,896,552 yuan Decrease of 16,552 yuan

Looking at the list on the right, comparing this year with last year, although the content has increased or decreased, the total amount has decreased by 16,552 yuan this year. The key lies in the transfer of the general reserve fund. (According to the trial budget regulations promulgated by the central government, the reserve fund should account for 1% to 5% of the total amount. The current general reserve fund of 95,388 yuan is still less than 2% of the total amount of 4,880,000 yuan.)

World Tennis Tournament Concludes, America Wields Power and Wins Doubles Championship Again

[Lord, Van Ryn, Cochet, Brown]

Women's Doubles Championship [Won by Great Britain]

Mixed Doubles Championship [Won by America]

London, 4th Telegram The 55th Wimbledon World Tennis Tournament, which has been going on for two weeks, concluded today. The singles final was not held, greatly reducing interest. America won a total of three championships, Germany won one, and Great Britain won one.

Men's Doubles Final Results

Lord, Van Ryn (USA) 6-2, 10-8, 9-11, 3-6, 6-3, Cochet, Brown (France)

Women's Doubles Final Results

Mrs. Shebalen, Miss McFord (England) (3-6, 6-3, 6-4), Mrs. Medasa (France), Mrs. Shegard (Belgium)

Mixed Doubles Final Results

Lord, Mrs. Haber (6-3, 1-6, 6-1), Collins, Miss Letley (England)

Two More Championships Go to America

After winning the men's singles championship, America won the men's doubles and mixed doubles finals today, and the championships went west across the Atlantic to America again. The French team of Cochet and Brown surrendered after a fierce battle.

Great Britain's Consolation in Disappointment

Great Britain's consolation in disappointment was that Mrs. Shebalen and Miss McFord won the women's doubles championship.

Wimbledon Tournament Concludes

The 55th Wimbledon World Tennis Tournament has concluded. The process was full of changes and worthy of pondering.

Formidable American Young Players Among the 250 players who joined, the most impressive are the 20-year-old American Hills, who won the men's singles final, and the 19-year-old Wood. The American youth are handsome and swept the world's heroes. The future of American tennis is probably unlimited. And Lord and Van Ryn's doubles are also invincible in the world. Thiel's prediction has not lost the hero's vision.

Astonishing French Rout The most astonishing thing is the complete rout of the French players. Cochet was defeated by the unknown hero Haber in the first week, Bausé was also eliminated in the fourth week, and Borough Chura was defeated in the semi-finals. The most promising doubles was also overcome by the Americans, and no one returned, which was unexpected.

Great Britain's Enthusiasm Dissipated This year, the British team had great ambitions to win the championship. The strength was the strongest in years. Players like Whiteley and Austin were ambitious, but unfortunately, both singles and doubles were defeated by the Americans. A burst of enthusiasm dissipated. The women's champion, Miss Nana, failed, which was the most heartbreaking. Fortunately, they still won a women's doubles championship in the end, which was a little comforting.

Japan's Strength is Still Far Behind Japan's strength is still far behind. Among the five players, Jiro Sato performed the best, reaching the semi-finals in singles before losing to Borough Chura.

Speaking of the Davis Cup Situation

With the Wimbledon tournament over, the Davis Cup final is about to begin. America's power and influence have suddenly increased greatly. Although Great Britain will definitely beat the Czech Republic, it is feared that they are still no match for America. The decisive battle between America and France will once again cause a worldwide sensation.
