Finance 125

Last Week's Standard Gold Price Hovered Around 700 Taels

Weekly Situation Saw Slight Increase: Last week, the standard gold price showed a slight increase again, the situation was exceptionally complex and chaotic, unstable and unsettled, fluctuating by ten taels at a time, and dramatically reversing by twenty or thirty taels. People were shocked and didn't know what to do. However, the storm was not as turbulent as the previous week, but still considerable. It was truly because the matter of the US-French war debt was brewing, the news was mixed, and the overseas silver market trended upward. Also, the Shanghai market exchange rate quotation lengthened by one and a half notches, perhaps because the actual transaction prices of the banks were collectively calculated and evened out, so arbitrage gradually approached. However, Chinese merchants frequently sold, still occupying short positions. As for the gold market, from the lowest price at the beginning of the week, it suddenly became 685 taels, and the highest price was 721 taels. Mid-week coincided with the bank's semi-annual settlement, with two days of holiday. After resuming, it hovered around 700 taels, with the upper limit around 710 taels and the lower limit between 690 taels. This week, there was a difference of 36 taels in total calculation, slightly increasing by one and a half taels. This was because there was a lot of arbitrage, but few promissory notes, and the bullish side was greatly hit the previous week, and they were unwilling to accept it, so they bought in again, hoping to pull it up. Perhaps the silver market and the exchange rate increased, but were unmoved. It is found that the current Dalian gang and Fu Chang Yuan Heng, and arbitrageurs are all in long positions, while the short positions are like Run Chang Xiang, Da Xing, Yong Heng Xing, etc. As for the spot goods, they were only collected and settled on the 3rd of this month (referring to those that had not been rolled over in July), totaling more than 20,000 notes. Yesterday, it was heard that there were still 7,000 or 8,000 notes, which had not been settled due to account transfer. The quoted price for day-to-day settlement was initially pressed down by more than 40 taels to around 30 taels, and finally more than 20 taels. As for the "red notes," they were increased by fourteen or fifteen taels compared to the standard gold price. Recently, the sales channels of Tianjin and other gangs were still active, and they were sold to them by Ying Feng Heng and other gold shops. However, the inventory is insufficient, or there is potential for an increase. Now, the general situation of this week is excerpted below.

Total Increase of Two and a Half Taels for the Whole Week: From Tuesday (June 29), the large promissory note increased by 375, the silver price rose by 625, the initial telegraphic transfer lengthened by one notch, and then shortened. The internal market was initially loose and then tight, and the trade had some collusion. Perhaps the gold market fell and then rose again, and storms arose, with a dramatic reversal of thirty-three or thirty-four taels. It opened early at 686 and a half taels, plummeted fifteen and a half taels, because France seemed to agree to the war debt, so people were fearful, and the sellers were strong. The next sudden increase was to 85 taels. Later, speculator Mr. Wu bought in, and the short sellers also covered their positions, so the price quickly turned to the peak. At noon, the HSBC quotation lengthened and then shortened, and then broke through the 700-tael mark, reaching 711 and a half taels. The afternoon was particularly strong, and buyers were like clouds, once rising to eighteen and a half taels. By the close of the market, it slightly declined, calculated at fifteen taels and eight cents, an increase of thirteen taels and eight cents compared to last Saturday. The next day, the large promissory note returned to a low of 0625, the silver price shortened by 375, and the telegraphic transfer remained unchanged, but the after-hours market was loose. The trade initially settled and then exited. The standard gold price opened down by four taels and eight cents, at 711 taels, actually because the Bank of England slightly contracted. However, the foothold was still good, and it immediately rebounded. Moreover, large clients competed to buy, and it was also reported that the French war debt matter was still under discussion, and people cheered up, and it suddenly soared ten taels, reaching 721 taels. Afterwards, the selling pressure surged, the exchange market seemed weak, plummeting by twenty taels, and then rising again, rising and falling constantly. The noon closing was 06 taels, and in the afternoon it reached 701 taels, and then 09 taels and eight cents. The Indian exchange rate turned small, and the telegraphic transfer was also firm. By the close of the market, it was 06 and a half taels, a drop of nine taels and three cents compared to the previous day. Xinzha: Yesterday, there were not many ships arriving from all directions, and the market was smooth. Buyers of Su and Chang thick japonica rice were particularly eager. The top-grade goods and the middle section each increased by one or two corners. At this time, when there are few goods and thin inventories, and the shops' appetites are also dull, the intention to enter the city is strong, and the price is raised again. Du Bu Jian is also gradually feeling withered. The arrival of early and late rice is slightly scarce. The inland and transshipment gangs have a slight movement. This street's appetite is focused on the various indica rice from the river. Because it slightly increased the day before, the buyers wanted to turn flat and then enter again, so it was once dull. Yesterday, the market situation suddenly changed, and it rose by one foot and a half following the thick japonica rice. Although glutinous rice was firm and stable, it had an upward trend. Yesterday, Taikoo Company's ships loaded a ship of foreign rice, totaling about 70,000 bags of Min Dang rice and small twisted rice. Customer gangs are not moving, and this street is only scattered. The market sentiment is mediocre.

Hunan, Shanghai: Yesterday, there were more than a dozen sources, and the sales market for each gang was very prosperous. Su and Chang thick japonica rice were quite stable at first, returning to the Zhabei rising trend. The opening price in the morning rose by one or two corners, with slight differences in the top and second grades. Ping Li white japonica rice was uniformly raised by a foot. The buyers' attitude is that the source before the Little Heat must be prosperous, so they only follow the entry and exit. Qingjiao Si Song thin rice has risen close to the corner, but the cargo customers are still unwilling to sell too much. Du Yangjian rice from the river is very withered, but there are still daily stocks. Free Talk

A Thought 145

— Autumn Waters

Love is like a roulette game. Or a speculative venture. If you want to protect your wealth, it's best not to get involved.

Husbands are like clocks. If you don't wind them, they'll rust and stop obeying you. But if you wind them too much, the spring will break and they'll stop working altogether.

In the old days, winning a woman's love and a kiss from someone of the opposite sex was harder than fishing. You needed real skill and patience. But nowadays, love and kisses are as common as chocolate, available anytime, anywhere.

Humans are imitative creatures. Ever since silent film star Clara Bow became famous, the earth has suddenly been filled with many charming women.

The incense and candles in the rainbow temple, the red turbans on the Sikh guards, the nighttime displays in the flesh market, and the scramble to touch Jinlong's hands are all unique features of Nanjing Road in Shanghai. First-time visitors must experience them to complete their trip.

Only fools believe that everything teachers say is gospel.

Facilities a Hotel Should Have 146

— Zui Chi Sheng (Drunken Fool)

My Opinion on Preventing Suicide

Recently, the number of people who, embracing a pessimistic view of life, decide to move on to another world is increasing daily, and they mostly use hotels as their final destination. Hotels are originally intended for travelers to rest and for men and women to meet secretly. They are designed for the living, not for the dead. But now they have taken on such a function, which the founders never expected. Therefore, if we want to prevent suicide, we must find a way to eliminate it from this base. Deeply saddened by what I have witnessed, I would like to offer the following suggestions for those who run hotels:

(1) Establish an Inspection Department: The Inspection Department should have one director, and one male and one female inspector. They must be sharp-eyed and good at observing people's complexions. Whenever couples or single travelers check in, if they appear abnormal or suspicious, they should be inspected one by one according to the "target shooting" method. Check for smuggled opium, sleeping pills, and other poisons. Once found, the poisons should be confiscated and the guests gently persuaded and refused accommodation. All hotels should follow the same procedure. When these people are repeatedly blocked, they will find it difficult to take action, and will naturally change their minds and abandon the idea of suicide.

(2) Post Numerous Slogans: I remember last year, because so many people were committing suicide by drowning in the Huangpu River, the Social Affairs Bureau erected slogans at various wharves along the river. Since then, it has been quite effective, and the number of suicides in the Huangpu River has decreased. Now, hotels can also follow this example. Various exhortatory slogans should be posted everywhere, in the halls, rooms, even the toilets, bathrooms, and on the bed curtains. Explain the suffering of the soul after suicide, and awaken the deluded. Those who intend to commit suicide, when alone and quiet, will be startled by what they see, and the fear of death will naturally arise.

If the above two measures can be implemented, the number of wronged souls in the city of the unjustly dead will surely be reduced. I piously put my hands together and pray, "Great Compassion, Great Mercy, Savior from Suffering and Calamities, Savior King Bodhisattva."

Predicting Weather Changes from the Form and Movements of Animals 147

— Ai Feng (Love Peak)

The Opposing Personalities of Dogs and Cats and the Weather: The ancients had a saying, "The hearts of men are as different as their faces," which feels quite stale. Also, commenting on people's incompatible natures is like comparing dogs and monkeys, which is also inevitably musty. However, there are still some interesting points.

When we observe the natural world and the human world, the phenomenon of dogs and monkeys living together is almost nonexistent, except for those who use monkeys for street performances. Moreover, even between parents and offspring, if they are placed in different locations for as long as a month, they will turn against each other and bite, as if they were enemies. This is something we often witness. It is only natural that dogs and monkeys, belonging to different species, should bare their teeth at each other. However, the ancients never compared dogs and cats, which raises questions for us. Dogs and cats can be seen anywhere and anytime, and their irreconcilable opposition is self-evident. Even their ability to predict the weather is different, which is truly interesting. For example, when a dog eats grass, the next day will surely be sunny; when a cat eats grass, the next day will be rainy. Although there are no numerical statistics on the accuracy of this phenomenon, it is more reliable than the saying that a horse's neighing indicates sunshine and a cow's mooing indicates wind. I firmly believe it is accurate.

The Form and Movements of Cows and Cats

(1) A Cow's Long Dribble Indicates Sunshine: The phrase "a cow's dribble is three thousand feet long" is undoubtedly an exaggeration. The length of a cow's dribble varies from day to day, a point that is often overlooked. This is also because the degree of use of the cow varies, such as the weight of the goods carried and the distance of the road. Moreover, it is not easy to judge by observing only a few cows. Therefore, it is necessary to pay attention to the weather on the day and observe many cow carts. If a cow's dribble almost reaches the ground, then the weather will surely be sunny. Based on the results of statistics over two or three years, this phenomenon is rarely seen except on very hot summer days unless it is sunny.

(2) The Way a Cat Washes Its Face: The action of a cat rubbing its face with its front paws is called washing its face. There are two forms:

1. The action is limited to the face, which is true face washing. 2. The action extends to the back of the head, frequently rubbing both ears, which is a special situation. The former indicates sunshine, and the latter indicates rain. As for the accuracy rate, it is difficult to say for sure, but it is at least more than half certain. However, the reverse phenomenon, that a cat will surely rub its ears before rain, is not necessarily true.

Statistics on "Tips" 148

— Autumn Waters

Tips, also known as "wine money," or, to put it more elegantly, "rewards." It is almost impossible to go to a social gathering without encountering the prevailing "tipping system." A few years ago, I heard someone say that their home had a telephone, and one year-end, a telephone operator actually asked for wine money over the phone, which shows how prevalent tipping is. No one in society dislikes it.

Recently, the British government conducted a "Tipping Census" in the hope of finding out the current state of this bad habit in society and trying to find a way to improve it.

According to the results of their investigation, the employees who receive the most tips are the porters in large hotels, followed by the male and female waiters in various hotels, restaurants, and other public places. The head porter of a large hotel in London and a head waiter at a certain place earn more than five pounds a week in tips, which is shocking. Other employees, such as waitresses, earn more than two pounds a week. Even the slowest business has at least five to ten shillings in extra income. These people regard tips as their only source of profit, and their meager monthly salaries are not in their minds.

London is a prosperous area of the world, so Londoners are often more generous with tips than others when they go to social gatherings. The most common example is "one tenth." For example, if you dine in a restaurant and the meal costs one yuan, you must pay one jiao (dime) in tips. The minimum limit is three pence for male waiters and two pence for female waiters. Outside of London, the tipping system is far less prevalent than in London. Americans used to have this system, but now they have improved it a lot.

As for our country, this bad habit is also prevalent in society. However, because there are no statistics to study, it is impossible to know the details. However, based on my ideal conjecture, the tea boys in major hotels and the male and female waiters in other public places must earn no less in tips than those in London. And under the special circumstances of Shanghai, the earnings of female waiters are much better than those of male waiters. The National Government once issued an order "prohibiting rewards," and it is hoped that people in society will pay attention to the spread of this bad habit.

A Record of Lotus Petal Rouge 149

— Zheng Yimei

The Avatamsaka Sutra states that in all the worlds of the Buddhas, the Tathagata is seen sitting on a jeweled lion throne made of lotus flowers. Therefore, the Buddha's throne is called the lotus throne. Wang Zian also wrote the line "The lotus throne has a divine countenance, and the pine cliffs retain sacred traces." The lotus flower stands tall and pure, naturally associated with immortals and Buddhas. I once said that a nude beauty in a giant lotus blossom would possess the beauty of jade-like purity and ice-like clarity. Unexpectedly, after indulging in such fantasies for a long time, I finally saw it in the "Oriental Nights" film produced by a Shanghai film company. During the banquet of King Amita, when the heroes were showing off their talents, there were all kinds of performances. And then, the lotus flower beauty slowly emerged. The lotus was as big as a niche, made of crystal paper, all clear and bright. This slender beauty modestly hid her breasts and looked shy inside. Then, when the mechanism was triggered, the lotus petals spread out and drooped, revealing her beauty. Then she gracefully began to dance and sing the songs of the day, her voice cold and crisp like jade, and her lotus arms and fragrant breasts made people's hearts flutter. This scene should only exist in heaven, and it is rare to see it in the human world. It is truly a feast for the eyes.

Miss Qiu Jin's Daughter, Wang Guifen, Returns from Studying Aviation in America (Part 2) 150

— Xu Wancheng

If she passed the doctor's examination, aviation organizations from various places would send her reference books for free, allowing her to study aviation in detail without spending a penny. Upon hearing the news, relatives and friends sent letters and telegrams, offering words of encouragement.

The United States has aviation police who have designated air routes. There are fixed routes to fly to any location. There are strict punishment regulations for flying on the wrong route, to prevent collisions and accidents.

American military aircraft often fly to the suburbs to practice dropping bombs, with a designated area on the ground. They drop bombs from high altitudes for practice. Every year, there is an airplane exhibition in Washington. That night, countless airplanes are decorated with electric lights, shining brightly in various colors. People from all over the country flock to see the spectacle, creating an extremely lively scene.

American airplanes are all equipped with airborne wireless telephones, and commercial airplanes can also listen to music. The sound is very clear through the two tightly fitted earcups. There are also weather stations in various locations specifically established for aviation.

American women are adventurous. In the hot summer, they often climb onto the wings of airplanes to cool off. This might be seen as a strange tale in China, but it is common in America.

The American government currently has a reward for "whoever can invent an airplane with the speed and force of a gun or cannon, traveling in a straight line, arriving in an instant." But it is unknown when this will be realized.

As I was saying goodbye and leaving, Mr. Huang Jingwan told me on the way, "Miss Wang's courtesy name is Canzhi. She loves martial arts and is skilled in boxing and sword dancing. When Americans have gatherings in America, they often invite her to perform, bringing honor to Chinese women. Miss Wang is resolute, brave, and revolutionary. She is good at drinking and can drink three or four catties of yellow wine without getting drunk. She is filial. After returning to China a few days ago, she immediately went to West Lake to mourn her deceased mother's grave." I am recording this here to let people know Miss Wang's character.

Rotary Club Novel

??? (13) 151

— Xu Zhuodai

"The first line, isn't it 'Have you been well since we parted?' I've removed the word 'parted' and replaced it with 'separated.' 'Have you been well since we separated?' Isn't that more elegant?"

"Extremely elegant! Thank you! Please go downstairs! You've been disturbing me so much that I can't do anything. At this moment, you might as well do it for me."

The lady listened and, without saying a word, walked to the door, stood there for a while, and then said:

"I won't come up, and you won't come down, okay?"

Ziliang immediately started writing, ignoring her. She finally went downstairs. Ziliang calmed down and had only revised half of the piece when he heard the lady downstairs calling again.

"Ziliang!"

How could Ziliang dare to answer? If he answered, she would definitely come up. So he remained silent.

"Ziliang! Come down!"

Ziliang thought: That's not good! Could it be that she's calling me down for dinner? This morning, she called me down for porridge. If I didn't go down, she would eat all the porridge. If it's time for dinner now, if I don't answer, I'm afraid I won't get any food again. So I have to ask her clearly.

"Ziliang! Are you coming down or not?"

"What's the matter?"

The lady didn't answer. Ziliang only heard a series of clanging sounds from below. It turned out that the lady was knocking on the rice bowl with chopsticks. This was clearly a signal for dinner. How ridiculous! She actually treated me like a cat or a dog. Ziliang didn't have time to think it over and immediately put down his pen:

"Is it dinner?"

There was no answer from below.

Ziliang went downstairs and saw that the lady had indeed started eating first.

"I asked you, why didn't you answer?"

"How can I talk with a mouthful of food?"

Ziliang saw two bowls of yellowish rice and three bowls of vegetables on the table. Looking closely, he couldn't help but get angry again:

"How annoying! Why is it always soybean sprouts! Is there no other vegetable besides soybean sprouts?"

He hesitated to eat.

"Soybean sprouts, I just asked you about them, and you said it was good, so I bought them!"

"When did you ask me?"

"I said, 'Stir-fried silverfish with kidney, is that okay?' You said yes. Stir-fried silverfish with kidney is another name for soybean sprouts!"

Business News 152

Juxinlou Qingzhen Muslim Restaurant on Wuma Road, Zhenfeng Street, declares: This restaurant was previously founded by Wang, who operated it diligently. However, it did not improve for many years. Last month, Wang had other plans, so he transferred the restaurant to Mr. Bai. Since taking over, he has made great efforts to renovate it. The upstairs is divided into a main hall and flower halls. The downstairs also has an auditorium, which is available for banquets and funerals. The restaurant treats customers thoughtfully and responds to every request. Recently, the restaurant has been very busy and has a hard time keeping up with the demand.

The Sanyou Industrial Society declares that its bath products are exceptionally excellent. In order to promote rational bathing, it is holding a major promotion on bath towels, bathrobes, and blanket towels, with a uniform 20% discount. Bed sheets, free cloth, and other fabrics and tent materials are also subject to a 20% discount.

The Sanmin Company declares that the Zhenqiu Knitting Factory at the intersection of Gordon Road and Xiping Road was founded by Mr. Liu Zhixiang, a Shanghai businessman. Its knitted wool and cotton gloves, scarves, socks, warm hats, etc. are all of high quality and low price, and durable. Therefore, since its products have been released, they have been sold at home and abroad, and have earned great honor. The Three Tigers trademark is especially wonderful. As a result, those who wholesale and order goods have been very enthusiastic.

The Liangchen Good Friends Society at Touji Bridge, Beijing Road, declares that the Zhang Zhenlu cursive calligraphy and Ma Henian landscape collaborative fan exhibition at the company's head office and the Liangchen branch in Doushi Street has attracted tens of thousands of visitors for several days. Each of the fans is sold at a low price of two yuan, and more than a thousand pieces have been sold. The exhibition lasts for only three days, and the exhibition hours are from 8:00 AM to 9:00 PM every day. If you call 12383, the company can send someone to deliver the items.

The Huashang Advertising Company declares that when Prince Wales H.R.H. was hunting in East Africa last year, he needed a reliable means of transportation. The Nali Baford Management Office provided him with a fleet of Ford cars and cargo vehicles for his use, and the result was very satisfactory.

Theater News 153

The Youlian Film Company declares that its new film, "Five Episodes of A Heroic Daughter," directed by Wen Yimin and starring Fan Xuepeng, will be released at the Central Grand Theater on the 8th of this month. Youlian Company began producing "A Heroic Daughter" in 1927, and it was the originator of martial arts films produced by Chinese film companies. The fifth episode is about the Thirteenth Sister's Great Destruction of the Fuhugang, which is the most critical part of the entire play. The essence of the play is concentrated in this episode, which is not to be missed.

The Dacheng Troupe declares that the day before yesterday was Mr. Xu Jinchang's 30th birthday, and a banquet was held at the Dacheng Troupe in the Shanghai Wuxi Fellow Association on Qipu Road. More than 300 guests attended. Mr. Xu is a well-known figure in the ticket circle and has been running ticket offices for many years. This year, the troupe was established, relying heavily on Mr. Xu's planning. The Dacheng organization is more complete than other troupes, and its reputation has long been established. It has become one of the famous ticket offices in Shanghai. In addition, its location is convenient, and the members are especially developed. For Mr. Xu's birthday, the troupe and the Shanghai ticket club were specially invited to perform Peking Opera. Starting at 5:00 PM on the afternoon of the same day, Ms. Fang Juanling first performed a sanxian folk opera, followed by magic by Ye Jiangu, Yao Jianhong, and Hua Aijun, followed by Peking Opera: (1) Mr. Fan Qichang's "Performing Good Deeds and Having a Son," (2) Mr. Lin Yonghua's "Ma Yi Saves the Lord," (3) The three gentlemen Fang Yiqi, Gong Yuanqiang, and Lu Shouzhi's "Going to Heaven," (4) Mr. Tao Chubai and Mr. Wang Baoqin's "Fen River Bay," (5) Ms. Fang Juanling, Mr. Lu Shouzhi, and Mr. Wang Shaowen's "Catching and Releasing Cao," (6) Miss Jin, Mr. Gong Yuanqiang, Mr. Wei Junbiao, Mr. Lu Shouzhi, and others' full-length performance of "Wulongyuan," (7) Mr. Ma Zhenwu and Mr. Wang Huisheng's "Wujiapo," (8) Mr. Wang Shaowen and Mr. Xu Hongshu's "Empty City Stratagem," (9) Mr. Tang Zhuping and Mr. Cai Rongxi's "Sipan Mountain." The performances of each play were very wonderful, with both singing and acting being excellent. The audience cheered continuously throughout the venue, making it an unprecedented grand occasion.
